@003 'JIGS MED STOBS BCU'I RGYAL THABS LA GNAS SHING, ,

'PHRIN LAS AA KshOO HI nI'I DPUNG RTZAL GYIS, ,LNGA BDO'I SMAG CHEN

DGRA TSOGS RAB BCOM STE, ,GDUL BYA RGYA MTSO 'DREN PA'I MGON

DES SKYONGS, ,THUGS BSKYED RGYA MTSO BSRUBS LAS LEGS 'KHRUNGS

SA BCU'I SHAR RI'I RTZER 'PHAGS TE, ,GANG 'DUL SKU YI GZUGS

BRNYAN BYE BA CHU KLUNG 'BUM DU RAB SPROS PA, ,BU RAM SHING BA

ZHES PA'I MTSAN GYI BDUD RTZIS RGUD PA KUN SEL PA'I, ,RNAM

'DREN BZHI BA SH'AKYA SENGGE 'BRAL MED GTZUG GI RGYAN DU 'DZIN, ,

GANG GI SANG MDZOD GSER GYI 'KHOR LO SGYUR MKHAS PA, ,MCHOG

ZUNG 'OD SRUNG KUN DGA' BO DANG NYE BAR 'KHOR, ,LA SOGS

DGRA BCOM 'PHAGS TSOGS BKA' DRIN CHES LCI BA, ,GSER

LDAN SGEG MOS THEG 'DI NGO MTSAR RMAD DU BYUNG, ,DED DPON

MKHAS PAS GRU RDZINGS LEGS BCAS NAS, ,BSAM 'PHEL NOR

BU DRANGS PAS RGUD PA BSAL, ,'JIG RTEN MIG GYUR SKAD GNYIS

SMRA BA YIS, ,MDO RGYUD RIN CHEN DRANGS PAS RGUD PA BSAL, ,

@004 RGYAL KUN MKHYEN RAB DMAR SER 'OD DU 'TSER BA'I NYI MA CHE, ,

NGUR SMRIG GAR DU RTZEN PA'I STON MCHOG SLAR YANG BYON PA BZHIN, ,

RGYAL BSTAN MTHA' DAG RMANG NAS GSOS PAS BLO BZANG RGYAL BA

ZHES, ,GRAGS PA'I SGRA CHEN SRID PA'I KHONGS LAS BRGAL BA GTZUG

TU BSTEN, ,DE YI SRAS MCHOG SKYE 'GRO'I GNYEN DANG RGUD MUN

DGRAR GYUR PA, ,RGYAL TSAB DAM PA DAR MA RIN CHEN MKHAS GRUB

DGE LEGS DPAL, ,LA SOGS MKHAS GRUB BRGYUD PAR BCAS

PA'I ZLA BRAL 'PHRIN LAS LA, ,RNAM PAR DPYOD PA'I BLO GROS LDAN

PA SU ZHIG GUS MI 'GYUR, ,KUN MKHYEN 'JAM DBYANGS BZHAD

PA ZHES GRAGS MKHAS DGU'I GTZUG GI RGYAN, ,'CHAD RTZOD RTZOM

GYI 'OD BRGYA 'BAR BAS RMONGS PA'I SMAG CHEN BSAL, ,THUB

BSTAN PAD TSAL BSKYANGS PAS BDE SKYID SBRANG RTZI'I DGA' STON

RGYAS, ,RDZOGS LDAN GSAR BA'I BYED PO DE LA BDAG SNYING RAB TU

GUS, ,DE YI SKYES RABS SKU TSE 'PHRENG BRGYUD SLOB DANG YANG SLOB

BCAS, ,'CHAD RTZOD RTZOM PA'I DPAL 'BAR RGYU SKAR GANGS LA 'KHU

BA YI, ,MKHAS DANG GRUB PA'I DPAL GYIS THUB BSTAN SPEL BA'I

RNAM PAR THAR, ,RO 'DZIN STONG DU SPRUL NAS BSKAL BRGYAR BRJOD

KYANG ZAD MTHA' BRAL, ,KHYAD PAR CHE RGU KUN GYI GTZUG GI NOR,,

'JIGS PA MED PA'I 'PHRIN LAS 'OD RLABS KYIS, ,THUB BSTAN

@005 PO BA RNAMS KYI BLOR 'TSAM ZHING GO SLA BA, GNAS LNGA RIG PA'I SNYING

BCUD 'DUS SHING 'JUG BDE BA, SHES LDAN RGAN PAS BKLAGS

NA BLO SKYED GSAR BA THOB PA, AA GSAR GZHON NUS BKLAGS NA

MOS GUS DBANG MED 'CHOR BA'I YON TAN GYI MDZOD CHEN PO ZHIG

YIN PAS, RGYA CHE'I KLOG PA PO RNAMS KYI DGE BA'I BSHES DANG BRTZE

BA'I GROGS SU GYUR CIG GU, ,

ZHES 'DI GA'I RTZOM SGRIG KHANG NAS,

SPYI LO 1996 ZLA 8 TSES 3 LA PHUL,

@001 SGRIG PA PO'I GTAM,

SLOB DPON CHEN MO DMU DGE BSAM GTAN RGYA MTSO MCHOG NI,

DENG DUS BOD MI RIGS SPYI'I GTZUG TU MCHOD PA'I MKHAS DBANG

CHEN PO ZHIG RED, KHONG GIS SKU TSE GANG BOR RANG MI RIGS KYI

RIG GNAS LA THUGS ZHEN ZAB BZHES NGOS NYAMS PA SOR CHUD, MA

NYAMS GONG 'PHEL, SHES RIG YAR RGYAS KYI DON DU BRTZE GZIGS

ZOL MED, BRTZON PA LHOD MED, GSUNG DBYANGS 'GAG MED

KYIS RANG NUS GANG YOD PHUL BA'I BKA' DRIN NI BSAM BRJOD YUL

LAS 'DAS PA ZHIG RED, LHAG PAR DU KHONG GIS NGA TSOR BZHAG

PA'I RIG GZHUNG GI SHUL BZHAG RIN PO CHE LA BLTAS KYIN BLTAS

KYIN MOS GUS MCHI MA RAB TU 'KHRIGS, BSAM BZHIN BSAM

BZHIN RIN THANG GZHAL DU MED PA SHES, NGA RANG TSO MI RIGS DPE

SKRUN GYI LAS KA BYED MKHAN ZHIG YIN PA'I NGOS NAS BSHAD NA, SLOB

DPON CHEN MO 'DI BA'I PHYAG RTZOM MTHA' DAG PHYOGS GCIG TU

BSDUS TE GSUNG 'BUM CHA TSANG ZHIG BSGRIGS NAS PAR DU BSKRUN NA

@002 NI RANG MI RIGS KYI RIG GNAS BANG MDZOD LA RIN CHEN NOR BU

ZHIG BSNAN PA LTA BU'I DGE MTSAN CHEN PO LDAN ZHING, LAR BLO

GSAL GZHON NU'I TSOGS LA RIG PA'I DNGOS PO PHUN SUM TSOGS PA

ZHIG MNGON PAR BSTABS PA'I PHAN YON SHIN TU MI DMAN PA ZHIG

YOD PAR MTHONG NAS DE LUGS KYI BRTZON PA LHUR LEN PA'I 'DUN

PA DRAG PO SNYING LA BCAGS KHAR, NYE LAM RJE NYID KYI SKU SRING BDE

MCHOG SKYID DANG KHONG GI YANG TSA GRVA BTZUN BSLAB GSUM RGYA MTSO

ZUNG GIS SA THAG RING BO'I DKA' SDUG LA MA 'DZEMS PAR RJE NYID

KYI GSUNG RTZOM MTHA' DAG DRE'U KHAL DU LONGS PA ZHIG DNGOS SU

KHUR NAS RANG RE'I DPE SKRUN KHANG DU SLEBS SHING, KHYED DPE SKRUN

KHANG GI RTZOM SGRIG SPUS TSAD LEGS PAS GZHAN SU DANG GANG LA'ANG

MA SPRAD PAR KHYED CAG LA GTAD PA YIN ZHES GSUNG 'BUM DPAR

SKRUN GYI DNGOS SHUGS DBANG CHA YOD TSAD NGA TSOR PHUL BA DANG,

KHYAD PAR DU NGED DPE SKRUN KHANG LA MA DNGUL GYI 'KHOS KA ZHAN PA

MTHONG NAS, GCEN PO'I GSUNG 'BUM PAR DU BTAB NAS

BOD MI RIGS KYI RIG GNAS LA PHYAR BA GRU 'DEGS KYI NUS PA THON

NA DE LAS CHE BA MED CES GSUNGS TE GCEN RIN PO CHE'I BRTZAMS

YON SKAR GCIG KYANG MED PA'I THOG DA DUNG GZHAN LAS ZHAL

'DEBS DNGUL SGOR KHRI GNYIS TZAM BSDUS NAS GUN GSAB KYI

@003 ROGS SKYOR BYAS PA LA NGA TSO SEMS 'GUL CHEN PO DANG SKUL MA CHEN

PO THEBS TE, GZHI NAS KHONG GI GSUNG 'BUM CHA TSANG ZHIG SGRIG

PA'I 'CHAR GZHI DNGOS BSTAR BYAS PA YIN,

DA CHA NGA TSOS PAR DU BSKRUN PA'I GSUNG 'BUM 'DI LA KHYON

BSDOMS POD DRUG TU BKAR, POD DANG PO NI GTZO CHER RNAM THAR

SKOR YIN, 'DI'I NANG DU NGA TSOS DE SNGA SUS KYANG MJAL MA MYONG

BA'I MDO SMAD BSTAN PA'I BDAG PO RJE BLA KHO RIN PO CHE 'JIGS

MED 'PHRIN LAS RGYA MTSO'I RNAM THAR LO RGYUS MJAL THUB PAR MA

ZAD, RTZOM PA PO RANG NYID KYI BYUNG BA LO RGYUS LAS MKHAS CHEN

DAM PA ZHIG THOS SBYANG GI STOBS GA 'DRA ZHIG LA BRTEN NAS 'TSAR

LONGS BYUNG BA'I TSUL LA RGYUS MNGA' LON CING RANG NYID LA SBYANG

STOBS CHE RU BSKYED PA'I SKUL MA THEBS NGES YIN, POD GNYIS

PA NI GTZO CHER GZHUNG 'GREL SKOR TE, 'DI'I NANG NAS RTZOM PA

PO RANG NYID NANG DON RIG PA'I MKHAS DBANG ZHIG YIN PA'I NGOS

NAS DENG GI 'CHAD GRVA'I GZHUNG KHRID KYI DKA' GNAD LA DMIGS

NAS TSIG DON GNYIS GSAL GYI 'GREL BSHAD GNANG YOD, POD

GSUM PA NI GTZO CHER LO RGYUS SKOR TE, 'DI'I NANG DU BOD KYI LO

RGYUS DANG RIG GNAS DAR TSUL GYI LO RGYUS SOGS BKOD YOD PAS,

NGA TSOS LO RGYUS 'DI DAG LAS RTZOM PA PO'I LO RGYUS ZHIB 'JUG GI

@004 PHUL BYUNG GRUB 'BRAS MTHONG THUB PAR MA ZAD, MKHAS PA GZHAN

GYI GSUNG NA MED PA'I LEGS BSHAD BTZO MA'I GSER LTA BU'ANG MI

NYUNG BA ZHIG ZIN RGYU YOD DO, ,POD BZHI BA NI GTZO CHER SGRA SNYAN

NGAG SKAR RTZIS KYI SKOR YIN, 'DI'I NANG DU SLOB DPON 'DI BAS

SROL RGYUN RIG GNAS KYI BSLAB BYA SO SO RGYAS BSDUS 'TSAM ZHING GO

BDE BA'I LAM NAS BKRAL YOD PAS LAS DANG PO BA RNAMS LA NYE BAR MKHO ZHING 'JUG BDE BA'I GNAS DAM PA ZHIG TU 'KHUMS SO, ,

POD LNGA BA NI GTZO CHER SUM RTAGS DAG GSUM SKOR YIN, 'DI'I

NANG NAS NGA TSOS RTZOM PA PO'I DENG RABS KYI KHYAD CHOS LDAN PA'I

BRDA SPROD KYI GZHUNG LUGS DANG LTA BA GSAR BA, LAG LEN GYI RIN

THANG LDAN ZHING NYE BAR MKHO BA'I BSHAD PA GSAR BA SHES RTOGS

BYED THUB PA YIN, POD DRUG PA NI GSUNG THOR BU'I SKOR TE,

'DI'I NANG NAS NGA TSOS RTZOM PA POS GDUL BYA'I BLO GANG LA GANG

'TSAM DU SBYAR BA'I SHES BYA SNA TSOGS, DRI BA DRIS LAN, CHAB SHOG

SOGS MJAL THUB LA, GSUNG TZAG TZIG LA SNANG CHUNG MI BYED PAR

ZHIB TU BKLAGS NA NI BYE MA'I GSEB NAS GSER RDO RNYED PA LTA BU'I

DGA' SNANG SKYE'ANG SRID DO, ,

MDOR NA, KHONG GI GSUNG 'BUM LA BRJOD DON ZAB KYANG

TSIG 'GREL GSAL BA, RIG PA'I GNAS LA 'JUG PA'I LAS DANG

@005 RGYA MTSO SPEL BA'I BYUNG BA DAG ,BDAG 'DRA PHAL BAS BSNGAGS

BRJOD YUL LAS 'DAS, ,'ON KYANG DAD DANG SNYING RJE'I BSOD

NAMS SPRIN, ,NGES 'BYUNG BYANG SEMS RLUNG GIS NYER BSKUL TE, ,

SA LAM RTOGS PA'I SGRA DBYANGS SHUGS 'BYUNG BA'I, ,SKYES BU DAG

GI GSOS SU 'GYUR RO SNYAM, ,ZHING SA GSHIN PO'I SA BON GRUNG PO

SMAN 'GYUR RO SNYAM, ,NYI GZHON GSAR BA'I RTZE DGA' RGYAS PA NA, ,

'DAB BRGYA BA YI GE SAR RGYAS PA LTAR, ,SNGON BSAGS BSOD

NAMS BAG CHAGS BRTAS PA 'GAS, ,DAD PA'I SPU LONG G-YO

BAR 'GYUR BA SRID, ,DE'I PHYIR TSUL 'DIR LUS NGAG YID GSUM

ZHUGS SO, ,

DE LA 'DIR MKHAS DGU'I GTZUG GI NOR BU MDO SNGAGS GRUB

MTHA' RGYA MTSO'I PHA ROL TU PHYIN NAS ZAB RGYAS KYI GDAMS PA THUGS

NYAMS SU BSTAR BAS GRUB PA'I GO 'PHANG MTHON POR SLEBS DE

@006 BRJOD PAR DKA' BA DON GYI SLAD DU MTSAN NAS SMRAS NA, ^ BLO GO

RDO RJE 'CHANG ZHES YONGS SU GRAGS PA RJE BTZUN 'JIGS MED 'PHRIN

LAS RGYA MTSO'I RNAM PAR THAR BA RANG GI BLOS DPAG TSOD TZAM ZHIG

RTZOM KHUL BYED PA LA, RNAM THAR SPYI'I SDOM 'GOD PA DANG, SKU TSE

'DI NYID KYI RNAM THAR RAGS RIM THAR CHAGS SU 'GOD PA, RNAM

THAR SPYI'I DON BSDU BA GSUM,

DANG BO RNAM THAR SPYI'I SDOM 'GOD PA,

PAn CHEN THAMS CAD MKHYEN PA BLO BZANG 'PHRIN LAS LHUN

GRUB CHOS KYI RGYAL MTSAN DPAL BZANG BO'I ZHAL NAS, GANG GANG

GDUL BYA'I MOS PA DANG 'TSAM PAR, ,GSANG BA GSUM GYI MDZAD

BZANG BKOD PA 'BUM, ,BZHED PA JI BZHIN 'CHANG BA'I NGO

MTSAR 'PHRUL, ,MKHA' KHYAB ZHING DU ROL BA BSAM LAS 'DAS, ,

ZHES GSUNGS PA LTAR, DPAG MED GDOD NAS LONGS SPYOD RDZOGS

PA'I SKU'I NGO BOR SANGS RGYAS MA THAG MDZAD PA GANG GIS 'DUL

DGOS KYI GDUL BYA RNAMS LA GANG 'TSAM GYI SKU'I BKOD PA DPAG

MED SPROS PAS NAM MKHAS GAR KHYAB KYI ZHING KHAMS THAMS CAD SKU

DANG 'PHRIN LAS KYIS KHYAB PA YIN MOD, RNAM 'DREN BZHI BA

@007 SH'AKYA SENGGE'I MDO SNGAGS KYI BSTAN PA RIN PO CHE SPEL BA'I SLAD DU

'PHAGS PA'I YUL DANG GANGS CAN GYI LJONGS SU SKU'I SKYE BA BZHES

PA'I 'KHRUNGS RABS 'GA' ZHIG RJE BTZUN BSKAL BZANG THUB

BSTAN DBANG PHYUG SOGS YE SHES KYI SPYAN LDAN DAG GIS BKA' LUNG

'KHRUL MED LAS BYUNG BA NI, 'PHAGS PA'I YUL DU RTEN 'BYUNG

GSAL MDZAD 'PHAGS MCHOG KLU SGRUB, RNAL 'BYOR GYI DBANG PHYUG

CHEN PO L'U AI PA, MKHAS MCHOG YON TAN 'OD SOGS PAn GRUB DU

MA'I SKYE BA BZHES PA DANG, GANGS CAN GYI LJONGS 'DIR GRUB

DBANG LHO BRAG MAR BA, MNYAM MED PO TO BA, RGYAL BA GNYIS PA

BLO BZANG GRAGS PA, KUN MKHYEN 'JAM DBYANGS BZHAD PA'I RDO

RJE, DNGOS KYI SKU GONG MA MKHAS PA'I MCHOG GYUR KHRI CHEN 'JAM

DBYANGS RGYA MTSO SOGS KYI SKYE BA BZHES PAR GSUNGS, DE DAG

LAS SNGA MA RNAMS KYI RNAM THAR RANG RANG GI RNAM THAR DU GSAL LA,

SKU GONG MA DGE BA'I BSHES GNYEN KHRI CHEN 'JAM DBYANGS RGYA MTSO'I

RNAM THAR NI MDO SMAD CHOS 'BYUNG LAS, LNGA BCU BA BLA GO'I BLA

SAR 'JAM DBYANGS RGYA MTSO NI, YAB BLA MA SKYABS DANG, YUM

MKHA' 'GRO SKYID KYI SRAS SU CHU PHAG LA 'KHRUNGS, MA 'KHRUNGS PA'I

SNGON NAS YUM LA BYA LAG RTZE NAS DUNG DKAR LAN GSUM GTONG

BA'I RMI LTAS BYUNG, DANG PO DUS 'KHOR GRVA TSANG DU ZHUGS, DKA'

@008 RAMS BAR DU SONG, 'DON BZANG BA'I TSAD DU BYED, TSOGS BSAGS RAB 'BYAMS PA'I MTSAN BTAGS BLANGS, DE NAS THOS

BSAM GLING MDZOD DU ZHUGS, 'DZIN GRVA KHA DOG DKAR DMAR DU

BABS, BSDUS GRVA, BLO RTAGS, GZHUNG DU THAL PHRENG YONGS

RDZOGS THUGS 'DZIN MDZAD DE PHAR TSAD KYIS MTSON BKA' POD LNGA

LA GSHIS PHYIN PAR SBYANGS, 'GREL CHUNG DON GSAL, MDZOD

RTZA, GRUB MTHA' RTZA BA GSUM THUGS LA BZUNG STE DUS PHYIS BAR

RGYUN TU SKYOR, SDE KHRI RIN PO CHE LA BSNYEN RDZOGS ZHUS, SO BDUN

PA LA CHAB LTAG MA GNANG, PHYI LOR RDO RAMS PAR BZHAG LO

GSUM GYI RING CHOS GRVA CHAG MED KYIS DPE GZIGS DANG, BSOD

GRAGS PA'I 'DUL BA'I RGYUGS PHUL, CHU YOS DPYID DAM BCA'

BZHAG LO DE'I DGUN GRVA TSANG DGE BSKOS MDZAD, SHING SPRUL NAS

KA MDO DANG, KHO TSE'I KHRIR LO RER BZHUGS, RDO RJE 'DZIN PA LO

BZHI DANG, RGYUD PA DANG TSA GAN PE SHING GI KHRIR LO GNYIS RE,

SLAR YANG RGYUD KHRIR LO GCIG AURGE DANG DMU DGE'I KHRI LO GSUM

RE, DRUG CU CHU KHYIR TSOGS CHEN DU KHRI 'DON MDZAD, CHU PHAG LA

RIGS GRVA BTANG BSTUN DGONGS KHROL GYIS MTSAN SGROGS DGON GYI

KHRIR BSKO BZHAG GNANG, SNGAR ZHIG MTSAN LAM DU BYA LAG RTZE NAS

GDUGS MANG PO BABS PA NYID NAS BZUNG BAS GDUGS BCU

@009 GSUM BYUNG BA CHOS SDE DU MA'I KHRI BYED RGYU BYUNG BAS DE'I LTAS YIN

'DRA ZHES NYID NAS GSUNGS SHING, LAN CIG BYA LAG RTZE NAS

GZAN GSHOG PA BYAS TE 'PHUR BA TSOGS CHEN 'DU KHANG GLO SGO LA

'THOGS NAS SAR BAB PA'I MTSAN LAM KYANG BYUNG SNANG, RE

GSUM PA SHING GLANG LA MTSAN SGROGS DGON NAS GSHEGS PA'I

GDUNG RUS LA YI GE BYUNG BAR GRAG GO ,ZHES GSUNGS PA LTAR

DANG KHRIR PHEBS SKABS KUN TU DBANG BKA' CI RIGS KYIS SKAL

LDAN RNAMS SMIN GROL GYI LAM LA BKOD PAR NGES TE, KHE TSANG SGOM

CHEN SPRUL SKU 'JAM DBYANGS MKHAS GRUB RGYA MTSOS RANG RNAM LAS,

BKRA SHIS 'KHYIL GYI GDAN RABS LNGA BCU BA RJE 'JAM DBYANGS RGYA

MTSO DMU DGE BKRA SHIS 'KHOR LO'I DGON GYI KHRIR PHEBS SKABS

KHONG GI ZHAL SNGA LAS 'JAM DBYANGS DANG RTA MGRIN GYI RJES GNANG

SOGS CHOS BKA' DU MA THOB STE RTA MGRIN GYI BSNYEN MTSAMS LA

BSDAD PAS DAM SRI 'GA' ZHIG GI SKED PA BCAD PAR GSUNGS

SO, ,

SKU TSE 'DI NYID KYI RNAM THAR SPYI'I SDOM NI, RJE BTZUN TZONG KHA

PA CHEN PO'I ZHAL NAS, DANG POR RGYA CHEN THOS PA MANG DU BTZAL, ,

BAR DU GZHUNG LUGS THAMS CAD GDAMS PAR SHAR, ,THA MAR NYIN

MTSAN KUN TU NYAMS SU BLANGS, ,KUN KYANG BSTAN PA RGYAS PA'I CHED

@010 DU BSNGOS, ,ZHES DANG, GUNG THANG BSTAN PA'I SGRON ME'I ZHAL NAS,

MANG DU GSAN PAS RMONGS PA'I DGRA LAS RGYAL, ,TSUL BZHIN SGRUB

PAS RTOGS PA'I BTZAN SA ZIN, ,RNAM DPYOD DPUNG BAS BSTAN

PA'I RU MTSON BSGRENGS, ,'DI DAG NGO MTSAR GTAM GYI SA BON

YIN, ,ZHES GSUNGS PA LTAR DANG PO GRVA RKYANG DKYUS MA'I LUGS

KYIS MDO SNGAGS RIG GNAS DANG BCAS PA LA THOS PA RGYA CHEN PO

MANG DU BTZAL BA DANG, BAR DU GZHUNG LUGS THAMS CAD GDAMS

PAR SHAR TE 'KHOR BA SPYI DANG BYE BRAG LAS THUGS BYUNG ZHING SEMS

CAN THAMS CAD LA MA BU GCIG PA LA SNYING BRTZE BA LTA BU'I BRTZE BA

SNYING RJE CHEN POS KUN NAS BSLANGS TE BYANG CHUB MCHOG TU SEMS

BSKYED PA, THA MAR NYIN MTSAN KUN TU NYAMS SU BLANGS TE NYAMS

DANG RTOGS PA GONG DU 'PHEL BA DANG THOG MTHA' BAR GSUM GYI DGE

TSOGS KUN KYANG BSTAN PA RIN PO CHE RGYAS PA'I CHED DU BSNGOS TE CHOS

KYI 'KHOR LO BSKOR CING, BYA BA LAS KYI 'KHOR LO'I SGO NAS

KYANG BSTAN 'GRO'I DON RLABS CHEN MDZAD PA STE BZHIR 'DU BA YIN

NO, ,

DANG BOR RGYA CHEN THOS PA MANG DU BCAL BA'I SARGA,

DANG BO THOS PA RGYA CHEN PO BTZAL BA NI, GZHON NU'I DUS

@011 NAS SNGON SBYANGS BAG CHAGS SAD, ,CES GSUNGS PA LTAR THUN

MONG SNANG TSOD LA'ANG SNGON SBYANGS KYI BAG CHAGS SAD DE SHES BRTZON

ME LTAR 'BAR BAS THOS PA RGYA CHEN PO BTZAL TSUL NI, KHONG STAG

GE TSANG GI MDUN NAS KLOG SLOB PA SOGS TSEGS MED DU MKHYEN TE,

LO GCIG GI RING LA BLA RNAM DANG, SMON LAM LNGA, RGYAN 'JUG

'JIGS BYED GNYIS SOGS TSOGS 'DON CHOS SPYOD TSANG MA THUGS

SU CHUD, DE NAS GLING PAD MA'I BLA SAR ZHES PA RDO RAMS PA

'PHRIN LAS RGYA MTSO DGE RGAN DU BSTEN NAS DPE GZIGS DANG DPE

KHRID MA CHAD PAR ZHUS TE TSOGS SU ZHUGS NAS BSDUS GRVA YONGS

RDZOGS TSOGS RGYUGS LA PHUL, AA RU HOR CHEN TSE 'PHEL ZHES PA'I

DGE BSHES LA 'GAG RING THUNG GI DAM BCA'I SKABS THOG MAR

BZHENGS NAS SANGS RGYAS 'PHAGS PA RTZOD GZHIR BZUNG STE RNAM

MKHYEN MI RTAG PAR RTOGS PA'I BLO DANG GANG ZAG GANG YIN DRIS

PAS KHAS LEN 'DZIN DKA' BA BYUNG, DE RJES 'GREL BA DON GSAL

DANG, GRUB MTHA' RTZA BA THUGS 'DZIN GNANG NAS TSOGS RGYUGS

LA PHUL, DE RJES BLO RTAGS DON BDUN CU BCAS TSOGS RGYUGS LA

PHUL, TSOGS CHOS 'GRIM ZHING RIGS LAM MTHA' CHOD PA SBYANGS,

BLO RIGS KYI TSOGS GLING GNANG STE RTAGS GSAL DANG, DAM

BCA' DANG BA 'DREN PA GNANG BAS GZUR GNAS KUN GYIS

@012 BSNGAGS BRJOD KYI ROL MO BKROL, DE LTAR TSAD MA RNAM 'GREL GYI

SKOR THUGS 'DZIN DANG, DPE KHRID DPE GZIGS SOGS LA GZHAN

DANG MI 'DRA BAR 'BAD PAS TSIG DON GANG CHA NAS LEGS PAR

THUGS SU CHUD, DE NAS RGYAN 'JUG GNYIS SNGAR NAS THUGS 'DZIN

GNANG YOD PA DGUNG LO BCU DRUG STENG GZHUNG RGYUGS PHUL NAS DGE

'DUN NYI SHU GSAR RTZOD BYAS, DE RJES SKABS DANG BO'I MTHA'

DPYOD YONGS RDZOGS THUGS 'DZIN GNANG STE TSOGS RGYUGS LA PHUL,

PHYIS SU YANG PAn CHEN BDE LAM, 'JAM SDUD GNYIS, RJE'I

BSTOD 'GREL CHEN MO, SPYOD 'JUG CHEN MO SOGS DANG, DBAL

MANG SNGAGS KYI SPYI DON, LEGS BSHAD SNYING PO, 'DUL SDOM

SOGS THUGS 'DZIN GNANG BA DANG, 'DUL BA LUNG CHA TSANG LA

@013 'GYUR ZHING, ZHES PA LAS 'PHROS TE MI RTAG PA DANG MI RTAG PA

MOL ZHIB RGYAS ZHUS PAR, SKYABS MGON RIN PO CHE'I ZHAL NAS,

SNGON CHAD DUS SKABS LEGS DUS MNYAM MED SGRUB KHANG BA, DPON

SLOB BYAMS PA, ZHOG DON YOD MKHAS GRUB, YONGS 'DZIN RIN

@041 PO CHE SOGS KYIS BDE LAM DANG 'JAM DPAL ZHAL LUNG RES MOS

KYIS STON DPYID ZLA CHOS RE GNANG BA'I SROL MCHIS, DA CHA BOD

YUL CHOS KYI ZHING SAR YANG MING TZAM YANG DKON PA 'DI RED PAS

DGON SDE 'DI TSO BSTAN PA'I 'BYUNG GNAS GNYIS PAR BYED DGOS

RGYUR 'DUG PAS RES MOS KYIS LO RE BZHIN MA CHAD NA LEGS SNYAM

PA YIN GSUNGS PAR, RJE 'DI BAS LAGS JI SRID 'TSO'I BAR

NYID KYI DGONGS BZHED LTAR BSGRUB CES ZHUS, 'DI DAG GIS NANG

THUGS KYI SRAS SU GYUR TE CHOS KYI RGYAL TSAB TU DBANG BSKUR BA SHES

SLA'O, ,DE BZHIN DU SGO MANG RIN PO CHE BLO BZANG TSUL KHRIMS RGYA

MTSO DPAL BZANG BO YANG BSAM SBYOR GNYIS KYI SGO NAS TSUL

BZHIN BSTEN TE ZAB PA DANG RGYA CHE BA'I CHOS BKA' SHIN TU MANG BO

GSAN, KHONG GIS CHOS MANG BO GNANG NAS BSTAN PA'I BDAG

POR DBANG BSKUR BAR DGONGS TE, DBAL MANG TSANG LA GSUNG

'BUM MANG BO'I LUNG YOD CES YANG YANG GSUNGS PAR BRTEN

DBAL MANG RIN PO CHE 'JAM DBYANGS BSTAN 'DZIN RGYA MTSO LAS

GSUNG 'BUM MANG PO DANG GZHAN DBANG LUNG MANG PO ZHUS NAS THOB

LA CHOS BKA' DKON PA MANG BO ZHIG THOB PAS BKA' DRIN CHE ZHES

BRIS 'DUG PA DANG, RDO RJE 'PHRENG BA'I DBANG GNANG SKABS KYANG

DE BZHIN GSUNGS, BKA' 'GYUR GYI LUNG GI SKABS SGO MANG RIN

@042 PO CHES DPA' RIS BSTAN 'DZIN 'PHRIN LAS CHED MNGAGS KYIS KHA

DAR DKAR SER CHE LEGS SRID DU RING BA ZHIG BSKUR TE BKA'

'GYUR GYI 'CHAD NYAN LA THUGS DGYES PAR YOD TSUL DANG DE BZHIN

PHYIS SU'ANG BKA' CHOS 'CHAD SPEL RGYA CHER GNANG DGOS TSUL

SOGS NANG NYAMS DANG SBYAR BA'I BLAB BYA MANG DU GNANG BA SOGS

NI BSTAN PA'I BDAG POR MNGA' GSOL BA'O, ,

'JAM PA'I DBYANGS GUNG THANG RIN PO CHE BSTAN PA'I NYI MA

LAS SNGAR GZHON DUS NAS CHOS BKA' MANG PO GSAN ZHING PHYIS

SU'ANG MANG PO GSAN PA DANG, AA MCHOG RIN PO CHE SOGS CHOS

'BREL GANG THOB LA BKA' DRIN DRAN PA'I DAD GUS TSAD MED PA

MDZAD, 'JAM DBYANGS CHOS DAR BA'I ZHAL SNGA NAS LAS SGRA DANG

SDEB SBYOR GSAN SKABS, SNGON NAS 'BREL BA'I MTSAMS SBYOR ZHIG

GIS SAM RJE DE NYID LA SKYON RTOG SKAD CIG KYANG MA SHAR GSUNGS,

GZHAN YANG PAn CHEN THAMS CAD MKHYEN PA SKU GONG MA DANG PHAN

TSUN BLA SLOB TU GYUR, KHONG GIS ZHAL NAS, THAMS CAD MKHYEN

GZIGS MCHOG GIS DPAL DUS KYI 'KHOR LO'I DKYIL 'KHOR ZHAL

PHYES TE DBANG BSKUR BZHES PAS GSANG SNGAGS ZAB MO'I BYIN

RLABS DANG 'BREL RLABS CHEN THUGS BSKYED SMON PA'I RGYA MTSO DANG

GCIG TU LAD MO TZAM YIN YANG NAN TAN GYIS BYED BCUG PA RGYAL

@043 BSTAN SPYI DANG KHYAD PAR 'JAM MGON RING LUGS DAR RGYAS YUN

RING GI CHED YIN NGES LA ZHAR LA MTHA' MED NGAN SONG GI GTING RDO

BDAG 'KHOR BA MTHA' CAN DU BSGRUBS PA RED SNYAM DGA' DAD

SHIN TU RGYAS SHING NAM DRAN RES KYIS KYANG BYUNG, BKA' DRIN DE

NYID STONG GSUM GSER GYIS BKANG NAS PHUL YANG GZHAL NUS MIN

ZHES GSUNGS, DE LTAR CHOS 'BREL GANG THOB LA DAG SNANG TSAD

MED PA MDZAD PA SOGS BSHES GNYEN BSTEN TSUL LEGS PA'I RMANG

GZHI YOD PA'I STOBS KYIS SKU TSE RING ZHING MDZAD 'PHRIN PHYOGS MED

DU RGYAS, SNYIGS DUS 'DIR BSTAN PA'I SROG BZUNG ZHING 'PHRIN

LAS MKHA' KHYAB TU RGYAS PA'I 'BRAS RTAGS KYIS BSHES GNYEN GANG

BSTEN LA DAM TSIG GI SEL MA ZHUGS SHING BSTEN TSUL MA LOG PAR

GRUB BO, ,'ON KYANG ZHI BA LHAS, MTHO LA PHRAG DOG MNYAM DANG

'GRAN, ,DMAN LA NGA RGYAL BSTOD NA DREGS, ,ZHES PA'I

MTSAN NYID TSANG BA RE GNYIS RES LOG PAR RTOG PA'I 'BRAS BU

MYONG STE KHYI RGAN KU CO CHE BA RANG PHUNG BER KA'I CHAR 'BOD DU SONG

RNYED TSUL NI, SNGAR DPON TSANG SOGS KYIS TSA KVAN BE SHING GI KHRIR

@044 'GRO RGYU'I GROS MGO BTON PA THOS 'PHRAL THUGS LA SHAR BA GSUNGS

TSUL NI, DPE SHOG LDEB GSUM TZAM YANG 'DZIN SKYOR YID PHEBS PA

ZHIG MI 'BYUNG ZHES DANG, GZHUNG LUGS LA SBYANGS PA'I SKAL BA LTA

CI KHA TON MAG MUG RE BYED RGYU'I BSOD NAMS YANG MI 'DUG PA NGO

@045 LHA TSOGS KHO NA BSTEN PA ZHIG BYUNG NA, ,ZHES PA LTAR SKYID DU

TSOR BA YOD PA ZHIG MTHONG BAS RANG YANG DE 'DRA ZHIG BYUNG NA SNYAM

@046 SBYOR GNYIS KYI SGO NAS TSUL BZHIN DU BSTEN PAS BYIN RLABS KYI

@047 'DAM DU BYING, ,ZHES BLA GO RDO RJE 'CHANG ZHES YONGS SU GRAGS

@048 GNAS NAS DBEN PA'I GNAS BSTEN TE SGRUB PA NYAMS LEN GYIS

DUS 'DA' BA ZHIG BYED DGOS DGONGS NAS, KHONG ZHANG STON RIN

PO CHER ZHUS PAS LAN DU, DBEN PA RE BSTEN NAS DGE SBYOR BYA

NUS NA KHO BO SHIN TU DGA' GSUNGS, REB KONG PHYOGS KYI RI KHROD

PA TSO SGRUB TSUGS BZANG BAS DE PHYOGS SU PHEBS 'DOD SKYES TE

KHONG GONG SA SKYABS MGON MCHOG LA ZHUS PAS LAN DU REB KONG YIN

DGOS DON MI 'DUG 'DI KA'I BKRA SHIS DGE 'PHEL DU BZHUGS

ZHES REB KONG PHYOGS SU PHEBS PAR DGONGS PA MA KHROL, MKHAN

RIN PO CHE NGAG DBANG DGE LEGS TSANG DANG, SGO MANG MKHAN RIN

SU BSTAR TSUL LAG LEN ZHIB GSAL ZHUS, AA KHU RIN PO CHE'I

GNAD TSANG BA GSHAR SGOM BYAS TE NYIN MTSAN KUN TU NYAMS LEN

@049 LA 'BAD PA GNANG, LHAG LHA DU MA'I BSNYEN PA BTANG BA'I GRANGS

KA RAGS RIM ZHIG BKOD PA NI, SGROL DKAR YID BZHIN 'KHOR

LO'I BSNYEN PA TSAR BZHI, GSANG 'DUS 'PHAGS LUGS LAN

GSUM, GSANG 'DUS 'JAM RDOR DANG 'JIG RTEN DBANG PHYUG

TSAR RE RE, BDE MCHOG LO HU BA LO GCIG GI KHONGS SU RGYUN BSNYEN

@050 RDOR, 'KHOR CHEN, GUR RIGS BSDUS, RNAL 'BYOR NAM

MKHA', RTA MGRIN GSANG SGRUB, DUS 'KHOR, MA H'A MA YA,

@051 PA RE RE BTANG GSUNGS, 'DI DAG NI RAGS RIM TZAM YIN LA

SKU 'DA' KHA'I BAR DU LO LTAR DPYID MJUG DANG, DBYAR DANG,

STON STOD BKA' CHOS BAR MA CHAD PAR GNANG ZHING, STON MJUG

@052 DPER NA, KHONG RANG NYID KYIS BRIS PA'I RNAM THAR SA BON LAS,

AOm SVA STI, 'DIR GLENG BAR BYA BA'I GTAM GZHI NI, SNGA SOR ZHIG

BYANG RGYUD BSTAN PA'I GSAL BYED LUNG CHOS YON TAN GYI GTER

MDZOD M'A THE ZI GRAGS PA RGYA MTSO BA KHU DBON GYIS NYID NAS RANG

@053 NAS THABS MED DU SA BON TZAM 'GOD NA, JI SKAD DU RJE BSTAN

PA'I SGRON MES, SGRO BTAGS CHU BO GYEN DU 'THOR YANG MKHA' LA

@054 SKYE BA YIN PAR NGES, ,ZHE SDANG 'DI YI CHE LUGS KYIS, ,SBRUL

GYI SKYE BA YIN PAR NGES, ,ZHES GSUNGS PA LTAR CHAGS SOGS DUG

LNGA SHAS CHE ZHING MKHAS BTZUN BZANG GSUM SOGS DAM PAS

BSNGAGS 'OS KYI YON TAN TIL TZAM YANG MI DMIGS PA BCAS KYIS

NGA'I SKYE BA SNGON MA ZHIG LA SKYES BU DAM PA ZHIG LTA CI, KUN GYIS YA

RAB TU BYED RGYU ZHIG KYANG GTAN MED, BAG CHAGS NGAN PA SAD

LUGS, SEMS KYI 'CHAR SGO, LUS NGAG GI BYED SPYOD GANG LA BLTAS KYANG NGAN PA THAG CHOD CIG YIN PAS SKYES RABS BZANG BO

SHA STAG GSAR BSGRIGS KYIS DAM PA RNAMS LA SKYES RABS KYIS SDIG

MA BSAGS, 'ON KYANG DPAL LDAN ZLA BAS, LAS KYI SHUGS NI

CHU BO'I RGYUN DANG 'DRA, ,LAS DBANG CHU KLUNG BZLOG PA RAB TU

RNAMS LA GDAMS NGAG KHYAD PAR BA BSTAN PA LAS, KHONG RIN PO

RIGS NI MTSAN MA DAG LAS SHES, ,ZHES GSUNGS PA LTAR KHONG

@055 GI MDZAD PA THOS BSAM SGOM GSUM 'CHAD RTZOD RTZOM GSUM GANG CHA

NAS SHES NUS SO, ,DE LTAR THOS SGOM GYI 'BRAS BU RTAGS MTSAN

GCIG SKYABS MGON RIN PO CHE'I SKU MDUN DU PHEBS PAR SKYABS

MGON RIN PO CHE'I ZHAL NAS, DE RING KHYOD 'DIR 'ONGS PA LA

BLTAS SAM MDANG NGA'I RMI LAM DU RANG GIS CHOS GOS SER PO DRI MA

MED PA ZHIG GYON, KHYOD KYANG GAM NA 'DUG MDUN DU BYE'U CHUNG

ZHIG 'DUG PA LA GZHAN ZHIG GIS MKHAS MCHOG YON TAN 'OD RED

ZER BA ZHIG BYUNG BA CI YIN NAM ZHES LAN GNYIS GSUNGS, KHONG AA

LAGS RIN PO CHE 'DI BAS GSUNGS PA, DE SKABS MA SHES MOD PHYIS

BSAM NA RAB TSES LCAGS BYA'I GNAM LO GSAR BZHAD LA SKU PHRENG

'DI BAR RAB BYUNG 'BUL BA'I GRAS THOB PA DANG, PHYIS TSIGS

SNGA MA DGE TSUL GYI BSLAB PA PHUL BA SOGS LA BLTAS SAM SNYAM PA

KUN RTOG LA SHAR, ZHES PA TZAM LAS MA GSUNGS MOD, DON LA

NI MKHAS MCHOG YON TAN 'OD KYI SKYE BA YIN PAR LUNG BSTAN PA

DANG, SKU TSE 'DIR YANG SKYE BO MANG BO DGE TSUL SLONG GI SDOM PA

LA BKOD PA DANG, 'DUL BA RGYA MTSO'I SNYING BO'I 'GREL BA SOGS

'DUL BA'I GZHUNG RTZOM DANG, BSLAB BYA GNAM RTZE LDING MA SOGS

@056 'DUL BA'I SKOR GYI CHOS BKA' MANG BO'I LUNG DANG BSHAD LUNG KHRID

SOGS YANG YANG GNANG NAS MKHAS MCHOG YON TAN 'OD KYI RNAM

PAR THAR BA LTAR BSTAN PA'I GZHI MA CHOS 'DUL BA'I BSTAN PA

DGUNG DU 'DEGS PA'I LUNG BSTAN PA YIN NO, ,LO KYA TUN LA

MJAL DU PHEBS NAS BDE MCHOG YAB YUM GYI THUGS DAM MDZAD TSE

MKHA' 'GRO MA DMAR MO ZHIG GIS CHANG THOD PHOR GANG KHYER TE BYON

NAS 'DI 'THUNG ZER NGA NI DGE SLONG YIN PAS CHANG 'THUNG MI RUNG

SNYAM DU MA GSOL BAR, MKHA' 'GRO MA DES PHYAG GIS MA NE'I 'OG

NAS BZUNG STE 'GRAM PA GTZIR NAS CHANG THOD PHOR GANG BO KHAR

BLUGS PA DE NAS BZUNG STE CHOS 'CHAD PA LA SNGAR LAS KYANG SHAR

SHAR THON PA DA LTA'I 'DI LTA BU BYUNG ZHES SNOD LDAN 'GA' ZHIG LA

GSUNGS 'DUG YANG DE'I SKABS PHYIR LAM SE THA ZI NAS PHYIR

'ONGS LAM DU RGYA MO BONG BU ZHON PA ZHIG GIS RJES ZIN NAS SHING

THOG DANG, DONG TZE SOGS GNANG STE SHIN TU DGA' NYAMS KYIS,

BAL MA LA SKYABS SU MCHI'O, ,SANGS RGYAS LA SKYABS SU MCHI'O, ,

CHOS LA SKYABS SU MCHI'O, ,DGE 'DUN LA SKYABS SU MCHI'O, ,

BLA MA DKON MCHOG GSUM LA SKYABS SU MCHI'O, ,ZHES LAN

GCIG RJES BZLOS BYED BCUG STE NUB PHYOGS SHIG TU SONG, PHYIS

SKYABS MGON RIN PO CHE NAS SU DANG AE 'PHRAD GSUNG, RGYU MTSAN 
@057 DE ZHUS PAS DE KA RED CES GSUNGS PHEBS, AA KHU RIN PO CHE THUGS

RJE CAN NAS GSUNG 'PHROS SU DRI BA GNANG BA LA'ANG DE LTAR ZHUS

PAS, NA TSOD CI 'DRA 'DUG GSUNGS PAR, NGA LAS CUNG MTHO

SNYAM ZHUS PAR, 'O BYED DGOS PA YIN NO GSUNGS PA LA BLTAS

NA dA K'I'I ROL BA'AM, ZHES PA TZAM LAS MA GSUNGS MOD KYANG SNGA

PHYI 'DI DAG GI SKABS SU RJE BTZUN RDO RJE RNAL 'BYOR MAS ZHAL

GZIGS PA YIN TE, GSANG RNAM LAS, GRUB PA MCHOG GI SAR

GSHEGS PHA MTHING BA'I, ,ZUNG 'JUG MNGON DU MDZAD PA'I

RAGS PA'I RTEN, ,HE RUKA: DPAL MCHOD PA'I SPRIN SPROS PAS, ,

RGYAL YUM MKHA' SPYOD DBANG MO MNGON SUM GZIGS, ,ZHES

GSUNGS PAS SO, ,YANG SKYABS MGON RIN PO CHE'I ZHAL NAS,

MDANG NGA'I RMI LAM DU RI KHROD GONG MA'I SGOM KHANG GSAR BA'I NANG

DU YOD PA 'DRA BA LA, MAL NAS YAR LANGS MA THAG 'DRA BA LA

GZIM DPON DKON MCHOG BSTAN 'DZIN NAS KHRUS CHU KHYER NAS

'ONGS, KHRUS BYAS PA DANG THUN GYI MGO BRTZAMS PAS NYI MA LHAG SHAR

BAS, NGA'I SEMS LA 'DIR RI MGOR SONG BAS DES SHAR SNGA BA

RED SNYAM SGO'I PHYI ROL TU SONG PAS NAM MKHA' SHIN TU DVANGS PA LA

SHAR PHYOGS NAS NYI MA SHAR 'DUG DE'I GZUGS BRNYAN NUB RI'I

MKHA'I MTHONGS SU SHAR BA LA DE YANG NYI MA JI BZHIN PA 'DUG LHOR

@058 BLTAS PAS BRAG RI MTHO ZENG NGE BA MANG BOS BSKOR BA RMIS, PHYIS

SU MKHA' 'GRO SNYAN BRGYUD KYI DBANG ZHIG DE NAS LO DER BTON PAS DER BLTAS PA AE YIN SNYAM ZHES GSUNGS YOD, LO DER

MKHA' 'GRO SNYAN BRGYUD KYI DBANG GSUNG YUL NI BLA GO RDO RJE 'CHANG

'DI BA YIN LA, DER BLTAS PA YIN SNYAM ZHES GSUNGS PA NI, RJE

'DI BA'I MDZAD 'PHRIN LUNG BSTAN PAR SNANG STE, KHRUS BYAS THUN

GYI MGO BRTZAMS PAS NYI MA LHAG SHAR PAS NGA'I SEMS LA 'DIR RI

MGOR SONG PA DES SHAR BA RED SNYAM ZHES PA NI, SKU TSE STOD DGUNG

LO SUM CU YAR MAR NAS CHOS KYI 'KHOR LO BSKOR BA'I MGO BZUNG

BA'I LUNG BSTAN DANG, SGO'I PHYI ROL TU SONG BAS NAM MKHA' SHIN

TU DVANGS PA LA SHAR NAS NYI MA SHAR 'DUG CES PA NI, BAR SKABS

SU MDO SMAD SPYI DANG, BYE BRAG BKRA SHIS 'KHYIL 'DIR HOS 'KHRUG

SOGS KYI RKYEN LAS DUS MI BDE BA BYUNG MOD, RJE 'DI BA RI KHROD

NAS DGON PAR PHEBS NAS YUN RING BSHAD SGRUB KYI BSTAN PA

BSKYANGS PAS BYIN RLABS KYIS RIM GYIS ZHI STE BDE 'JAGS SU SONG

BAS MDO KHAMS SHAR PHYOGS 'DIR RGYAL BSTAN NYIN MO LTAR GSAL

BAR MDZAD PA DANG, DE'I GZUGS BRNYAN NUB RI'I MKHA'I

MTHONGS SU SHAR BA LA DE YANG NYI MA JI BZHIN 'DUG GSUNGS PA NI,

NUB PHYOGS DBUS GTZANG GI SANGS RGYAS BSTAN PA'I BDAG PO PAn

@059 CHEN SKU PHRENG SNGA PHYI GNYIS SOGS BSTAN 'DZIN DU MA SLOB MAR GYUR

BA DANG, MDO STOD KHAMS PHYOGS KYI LAB MKHAN CHEN DANG, ZUR MANG KUN KHYAB SOGS BSTAN 'DZIN DU MA SLOB MAR GYUR TE

BSTAN RGYUN MDO DBUS GTZANG GSUM DU KHYAB PA'I LUNG BSTAN

DANG, LHOR BLTAS PAS BRAG RI MTHO ZENG NGE BA MANG POS BSKOR

BA RMIS GSUNGS PA NI, MTHAR LHO PHYOGS KYI YUL GRU CHEN PO DAG

GI MI RIGS RNAMS KYIS SRID LA DBANG SGYUR BA'I LUNG BSTAN DU

NGES SO, ,YANG 'JIGS BYED GZHI BSNYEN CHEN MOR BZHUGS

SKABS, NANG GCIG THUN DANG BO GROL 'PHRAL KHA BA PHYAGS PHYIR RA

BAR PHEBS PAS SPYIL BU'I G-YON ZUR NGOS 'JA' TSON KHA DOG

DMAR PO GSAL DVANGS ZLUM PO ZHIG 'DUG PA LA YA MTSAN KHA BA SA

LA CHAGS PAS 'JA' SHAR BA 'DUG SNYAM RING ZHIG BLTAS PAS

'PHRAL MIG 'DZUM GCIG LA GLO BUR DU MED SONG ZHES GSUNGS 'DUG

DE YANG 'JA' RANG 'GA' BA ZHIG MIN PAR DAG PA'I GZIGS SNANG

KHYAD PAR BA ZHIG YIN PAR NGES TE GSANG RNAM LAS, 'JIGS

MDZAD RDO RJE'I RIM GNYIS RNAL 'BYOR MTHUS, ,ZHI KHRO RAB

'BYAMS BGRANG YAS DKYIL 'KHOR LHA, ,DAG PA'I BRTAN G-YO'I

BKOD PA 'BUM SHAR BAS, ,DMAR BO'I MDANGS 'DZIN 'OD KYI

GUR KHYIM GZIGS, ,ZHES GSUNGS, MKHA' SPYOD MA'I BSNYEN

@060 CHEN SKABS, SROD THUN LA RKYEN MED PAR GTING NAS NGU SNYING ZHIG

'ONGS NAS MANG PO NGUS, ,PHYI NYIN NYI DROS TZAM NA SKYABS MGON

NAS GNANG BYUNG ZER BA GCIG 'BYOR BA LA BLTAS PAS, SRID

DANG ZHI BA RO MNYAM NYID GYUR PA'I, ,SGRIB BRAL ZAG MED YE SHES

CHOS KYI SKU, ,THABS SHES MNYAM PAR SBYOR BA'I DGA' BDE YIS, ,NGO MTSAR GANG DE RDO RJE 'CHANG GI 'PHRUL, ,ZHES PA 'DUG PAS

SNGA GONG GI DE YANG SEMS SUN PA MIN NGES SHAR, ZHES GSUNGS,

SNGA GONG GI DGONG MO RKYEN MED PAR GTING NAS NGU SNYING 'ONGS NAS

MANG BO NGUS PA DE YANG, SEMS SUN SNANG SKYES NAS NGUS PA ZHIG

MIN NGES SHAR ZHES DON GYIS RTOGS PA ZHIG SKYES PA ZHAL KYIS BZHES

'DUG LA, SKYABS MGON THAMS CAD MKHYEN PA'I GSUNG RIS LA

BLTAS NA, SRID ZHI MNYAM NYID KYI CHOS SKU DANG, THABS BDE BA

CHEN PO'I YE SHES MNYAM PAR SBYOR BA'I BDE STONG DBYER MED KYI YE

SHES THUGS RGYUD LA 'KHRUNGS PAR NGES TE, DPAL LDAN ZLA BAS,

NANG DU RAB TU DGA' BA YANG DANG YANG DU 'BYUNG, ,RAB TU

DGA' BA LAS BYUNG MCHI MAS MIG BRLAN ZHING, ,LUS KYI BA SPU

LDANG BAR 'GYUR BA GANG YIN PA, ,DE LA RDZOGS PA'I SANGS RGYAS

BLO YI SA BON YOD, ,CES GSUNGS PA LTAR RTOGS PA KHYAD PAR BA

RE RGYUD LA SKYES TSE DGA' BA'I DBANG GIS MCHI MAS MIG BRLAN BA

@061 DU MA YOD DO, ,YANG GSUNG LAS, BAR SKABS SHIG MNAL LAM

DU BRAG DMAR BO ZHIG GI SKED NA 'PHRED LAM ZHIG YOD PAR PHYIN

PAS THUGS RJE CHEN PO'I 'PHRIN LAS LA BAR DU GCOD PA'I DAM

SRI RED SNYAM PA SKYA BTZUN GNYIS YOD PA'I SKYA BO DES DANG BOR MI

DGA' ZHING BRNYAS THABS BYED KYANG PHYI NAS MGO BOS BTUD, DE

NAS BTZUN GZUGS DES BDAG LA CHES CHER BRNYAS SHING 'PHYA BA LA

MA 'DZEM PAR PHYIN PAS BRAG PHUG CIG NA THUGS RJE CHEN PO MI PHAL

GYI LUS TSAD LAS NYIS 'GYUR GYI CHE BA'I SKU DVANGS GSAL, DAR

MTHING GI NA BZA' DANG DAR THOD CAN ZHIG BZHUGS PA LA TSAD MED

PA'I DAD PA ZHIG SKYES TE BDAG BLA NA MED PA'I BYANG CHUB MYUR DU

THOB PA ZHIG MKHYEN ZHUS PAR, YONG GSUNGS, BSAM NGO LA TSE

'DI'I SNANG SHAS TZAM YANG KHA MA BRI, NYON MONGS MGO RGOD DU

'DUG PAS NYON MONGS PA'I SPYOD TSUL 'DIS DE'I BAR JI 'DRA YONG

SNYAM 'JIGS ZHUM PA ZHIG BYUNG NAS, JI LTAR YANG LAS NYON GYI

'KHOR BA 'DI BZLOG THUB PA ZHIG CIS KYANG MKHYEN ZHUS PAR, YONG

GSUNGS, NGED PHYIR THON NAS BRAG DE'I STENG DU PHYIN NAS GNAS

PA LA, SKABS SHIG THUGS RJE CHEN PO DE PHYI ROL TU PHEBS BYUNG,

DAD PA TSAD MED PA ZHIG SKYES, DNGOS PO ZHIG 'DI LA 'BUL RGYU

YOD NA CI MA RUNG SNYAM PAS GZHAN MED KYANG LAG TU JA PHOR BA

@062 GANG YOD PA DE PHUL BAS, PHYAG YAR BSKYANGS TE BSNAMS YONG

PAS DGA' DAD CHES CHER SKYES PA ZHIG RMIS, SPYAN RAS GZIGS

KYI SKU'I RNAM PA YI GE PHYED DANG BZHI BA BYA BA ZHIG YOD PA DE DANG

MTHUN, RMI LAM GYI BAB SKYABS MGON GONG MA DE DANG 'GRIG PA

BYUNG, ZHES GSUNGS PA YANG BSAM GYIS MI KHYAB PA'I RNAM THAR

ZHIG YOD PAR NGES MOD ZHIB PAR SHES DKA' LA, SPYAN RAS

GZIGS KYI ZHAL MNGON SUM BSTAN PA YIN TE GSANG RNAM LAS,

MNAL DANG 'OD GSAL 'DRES PA'I NYAMS SNANG LA, ,SNYING RJE'I

GTER CHEN 'PHAGS MCHOG SPYAN RAS GZIGS, ,RGYA JAS MCHOD

CING GANG GANG GSOL BTAB PA, ,DE DE BZHIN DU 'GRUB CES

GSAL BAR GSUNGS, ,ZHES GSUNGS SO, ,YANG KHONG GIS

GSUNGS PA, NUB GCIG MNAL LAM DU RI ZHIG GI STENG NA STENG

'OG PHYOGS MTSAMS THAMS CAD SHEL GYI RANG BZHIN CAN RTZE BCU

DRUG PA ZHIG 'DUG PA LA MI ZHIG GIS STENG DU SONG DANG STONG GSUM

GYI BKOD PA THAMS CAD MTHONG NGO ZER, RTZE BCU BZHI BAR

PHYIN TE BLTAS PAS KHOR YUG KUN SMUG TENG NGE BA LA RI'I PHRENG BA RE

SPEL BAR YOD PA LAS GZHAN MA MTHONG, DA DUNG STENG DU SONG

DANG JE GSAL DU 'GRO ZHES NAN CHE BA BYAS KYANG YOM YOM G-YO BAS

'GRO MA NUS PAR RI'I PHAG NA RGYAL SRAS SKU MCHED GSUM BZHUGS

@063 PA MJAL DU PHYIN, PHU CHUNG BA YIN RGYU DES CANG MI GSUNG, SPYAN

SNGA BAS DGE BSHES 'DI LA MJOL GSUNGS, PO TO BA DANG YANG MJAL,

MNAL SAD PA DANG RDO RJE 'CHANG DANG ZUNG 'JUG GI THIG

LE MJAL MA NUS PA BSOD NAMS RE CHUNG SNYAM YANG ZHIB PAR BSAM

PAS DE DANG MTSUNGS PA BYUNG SNYAM PA LOG PA'I 'KHRUL NGOR SHAR,

PO TO BA SKYABS MGON 'KHRUNGS RABS NA BZHUGS PAS MGO BO

GTUGS TZAM MIN PAR SEL MA SHOR BA DGOS PA GO, ,PHYIS SKYABS

MGON SKU 'DA' BAR NYE BA'I SNGON DER ZHAL NAS, SKU ZHABS SKU

TSE PHRENG BRGYUD LA 'KHON MA ZHUGS PA ZHIG YIN TSE CHOS RGYUN DE KHO

RANG GIS THOB 'DUG NA SPYOD PA RTZING YANG MNYAN PAS CHOG 'KHON

ZHUGS YOD NA SEL BYA BA DE LA ZER BAS MNYAN GSUNGS PAS ZING

CHA MANG BO BYUNG SKABS KYANG GANG YIN GYI ZER RJES BSNYEGS TE RANG

PHUNGS GZHAN PHUNGS MA BYAS PA'ANG DE TSOS YIN, ZHES GSUNGS,

'DI SKABS KYI MNAL DANG 'OD GSAL 'DRES PA'I NYAMS LA RI

SHEL GYI RANG BZHIN RTZE MO BCU DRUG PA GSUNGS PA NI, BKA'

GDAMS THIG LE BCU DRUG GI NYAMS LEN LA GZHOL BAR MDZAD NAS

ZUNG 'JUG CHOS SKU'I THIG LE MNGON DU GYUR BAS BKA' GDAMS SKU

MCHED GSUM DANG DNGOS SU MJAL BA YIN TE GSANG RNAM LAS, LHA

CHOS BDUN LDAN ZUNG 'JUG THIG LE'I CHOS, ,ZAB GSAL GNYIS

@064 MED LHA YI RNAL 'BYOR GYIS, ,ZUNG 'JUG CHOS SKU'I THIG LE MNGON

GYUR BAS, ,SKU MCHED GSUM GYIS DGYES PA'I DBUGS DBYUNG

MDZAD, ,CES GSUNGS SO, ,YANG SKABS SHIG RGAN GYA'I BRAG

DKAR LA GNAS MJAL DU PHEBS, GNAS KHANG NAS RDO KHA SHAS KHYER

YONG BA LAM DU CHU LA STENG GI 'DAM BKRUS PAS, NUB MO RMI LAM DU

RDO DE RNAMS BKRUS PA'I 'DAM PHYE RNAMS SANGS RGYAS BYANG SEMS

KYI SKU GZUGS SHA STAG TU CHU LA G-YENG PA'I RMI LTAS BYUNG ZHES

GSUNGS PA YANG, GANG SNANG LHA SKUR 'CHAR BA'I RTOGS PA BRNYES

PA DANG, YANG MTSAN LAM DU MKHA' 'OD DVANGS GSAL GYI RANG

BZHIN NA LHA DANG LHA MO 'PHAN DANG RGYAL MTSAN THOGS PA MANG PO

SHAR PHYOGS SU 'GRO BA'I RJES NA LAB LUNG SKYABS MGON RED ZER

BA'I 'JA' 'OD KYI RANG BZHIN DVANGS GSAL SGRIB MED LA SKU

MDANGS SMUG PO GDONG ZOR BA, PHYAG G-YAS KYIS RANG GI KHA t'Am KA

'PHAN CHUNG G-YER KHA CAN ZHIG YOD PA BSNAMS NAS MKHA' LA SHAR

DU 'GRO BA ZHIG RMIS, DE GNAS BYIN RLABS CHE NGES SU 'DUG CES

GSUNGS PA YANG BRAG DKAR DE 'KHOR LO BDE MCHOG GI GNAS YIN

PAS BDE MCHOG GI ZHAL GZIGS PAR MNGON MOD ZUR TZAM LAS

MI GSUNGS 'DUG RJES SOR SHEL DGON DU BZHUGS SKABS NAM

GUNG MA LON TZAM NA GAM 'KHOD GRVA CHUNG ZHIG RA BAR PHYIN PAS

@065 GNAS RI'I RTZE NAS 'JA' TSON NYIS RIM ZHIG SHAR BA'I SNE KHONG

BZHUGS GNAS KYI GZIMS KHANG STENG DU ZUG PA MTHONG PA BZHIN RI

KHROD PA RNAMS KYIS KYANG MTHONG, MKHA' NGOS 'JA' TSON DRA BA

'OD LJANG KHUS KHEBS, SHEL DGON NAS PHEBS PA'I NANG PAR

BCIBS THOG NAS NYI ZLA SKAR GSUM KHONG NYID DANG ZHABS 'BRANG

THAMS CAD KYIS MTHONG, ZHAL NAS NYI ZLA SKAR GSUM DUS GCIG

LA 'DZOMS PA RTEN 'BREL LEGS ZHES GSUNGS, DE NAS RIM GYIS

PHEBS PAR SNGAR SHEL DGON GYI GNAS RI NAS 'JA' SHAR BA DE RJE

NYID KYI PHYI BZHIN 'BRANG STE 'ONGS PA KUN GYIS MTHONG, ZHAL NAS

DA 'GROR MI 'JUG KA GSUNGS NAS BCIBS LAS BABS STE DE

PHYOGS SU PHYAG GNANG ZHING RKANG BRGYAD SOGS GSUNGS, DE SKABS

'JA' DE KHONG NYID KYI PHYOGS SU GCIG DANG, PHAR PHYOGS SU

GCIG CHAD DE CHA GNYIS SU GYUR, DE NAS PHEBS PAS YANG 'JA'

GNYIS MTHUD DE SNGAR BZHIN 'ONGS PA SOGS LTAS YA MTSAN PA MANG

PO BYUNG BA MA DANG MKHA' 'GRO'I SKYEL MA GNANG BA RED DO, ,BYA

KHYUNG DU CHOS RJE DON 'GRUB RIN CHEN GYI GSER GDUNG ZHIG GSO'I

SKABS BDUD RTZI BABS PA KUN GYIS MTHONG, AA RA PA TZA NA'I SGRUB

PHUG TU BZHUGS SKABS AA RANG BYON ZHIG KYANG BYUNG, YANG SOG

PO'I 'DUS RI'I RTZER PHEBS SKABS MKHA' NGOS 'JA' TSON GYIS

@066 SBREL BA DANG NYI ZLA SKAR GSUM DUS GCIG TU SHAR BA KUN GYIS

MTHONG ZHING, RMA CHEN GYI GANGS RI DE NYID 'KHOR LO BDE MCHOG

GI PHO BRANG YIN PA LA RMA CHEN SGO SRUNG GI TSUL DU YOD PA GZIGS,

DGA' DAD SPRO GSUM DANG BYAMS SNYING RJE'I DBANG GIS SPYAN CHAB

RGYUN RING BSIL, GSANG RNAM LAS, 'DUS RI ZHES GRAGS SA

'DZIN DBANG PO'I RTZER, ,PHYI BLTAS LHUN CHAGS GANGS RI'I RNAM PA LA, ,NANG DU 'KHOR LO SDOM PA'I PHO BRANG GI, ,SGO SRUNG TSUL

DU RMA RGYAL BZHUGS PA GZIGS, ,ZHES GSUNGS SO, ,YANG PAn

CHEN RIN PO CHE SKU GONG MA BLA BRANG NAS YAR KHAMS PHYOGS SU PHEBS

ZIN SKABS SHIG KHONG GI ZHAL NAS, MDANG NGA'I RMI LAM DU PAn

CHEN RIN PO CHE RUS RGYAN MNABS NAS PHEBS TE DUNG DKAR ZHIG

GNANG NAS 'DI BDAG GYIS ZHES GSUNGS PA ZHIG RMIS GSUNGS,

NYE GNAS KYIS, PAn CHEN RIN PO CHES KHONG GI GSUNG 'BUM BDAG

GYIS ZHES PA'I BRDA RED PA ZHES ZHUS PAS, KHONG GIS MA RED

SPRUL SKU BDAG GYIS GSUNGS PA RED CES GSUNGS, DE NAS MA

'GOR BAR PAn CHEN THAMS CAD MKHYEN PA SKU 'DA' TSUL BSTAN

PA'I GLOG 'PHRIN 'BYOR, YANG SKYABS MGON BSTAN PA'I RGYAL

MTSAN SKU 'DA' TSUL BSTAN NAS ZLA DRUG GI MTSAMS SU KHONG GIS

GSUNG PA, MDANG NGA'I RMI LAM DU MTSO CHEN PO ZHIG GI KHA NA SPRUL

@067 SKU CHUNG CHUNG ZHIG 'DUG PAn CHEN RIN PO CHE YIN RGYU BYED KYANG NGA'I

BSAM PAR SKYABS MGON YIN SNYAM, ZHABS ZHU 'GA' 'DUG KYANG

GLING SPRUL SOGS MA RED, SPRUL SKUS MTSO KHAR NA BZA' DANG SKU 'DRA

ZHIG BKRU BZHIN PHAR PHEBS TSUR PHEBS BYAS NAS BZHUGS 'DUG

MTSO DE'I NANG KHA DOG MI 'DRA BA'I MTSO SNA LNGA DBUS DANG PHYOGS

BZHIR YOD, MTSO DE'I RGYA KHYON SKU 'BUM DANG BLA BRANG GI BAR GYI SA

KHYON LTA BU RGYA CHE BA'I NANG DU 'DOD YON LNGA SOGS MKHO DGU'I

DPAL 'BYOR BSAM GYIS MI KHYAB PAS GTAMS 'DUG MTSO DE LAG

TU BLANG NA BLANG CHOG LA, BZHAG NA BZHAG CHOG PA ZHIG RMIS ZHES

GSUNGS PA YANG PAn CHEN THAMS CAD MKHYEN GZIGS MCHOG GI

YANG SPRUL RIN PO CHE LA CHOS BKA' MANG BO PHUL TE BDAG GIR BZHES

PA DANG, SKYABS MGON MCHOG SPRUL RIN PO CHE 'DI BA 'KHRUNGS YUL

DANG MDZAD PA SOGS LUNG GSAL BOR BSTAN PA SOGS MA 'ONGS

MNGON SUM DU GZIGS PA'I 'BRAS RTAGS SHIG TU MNGON, 'DI DAG

NI RAGS RIM TZAM YIN LA GSANG RNAM LAS, SHEL DGON BDE CHEN

CHOS KYI PHO BRANG DU, ,RIM GNYIS ZAB MO'I RNAL 'BYOR LA GZHOL

BAS, ,HE RU KA DPAL MKHA' SPYOD DBANG MO SOGS, ,GANG SNANG

DAG PA'I ROL BA 'BYAMS SU KLAS, ,ZHES GSUNGS PA LTAR RO, ,

SMRAS PA, MNOG CHUNG SRID PA'I MCHING BU YONGS DOR

@068 NAS, ,BYANG CHUB SEMS KYI GRU RDZINGS LEGS PAR BSDAMS, ,RAB

DBEN RIN CHEN 'BYUNG GNAS LA ZHUGS TE, ,ZUNG 'JUG NOR

BU LEN MKHAN KHYOD MIN SU, ,MI GTZANG DRI LA ZHEN PA'I NAG CHUNG

SBRANG, ,RAB GTZANG PADMA'I TSAL LA MI GNAS BZHIN, ,BDE

MED SRID PAR ZHEN PA'I SKYE BO DAG ,BDE CHEN THAR BA'I LAM DANG

RING DU BRAL, ,ZAB GSANG RDO RJE'I RNAL 'BYOR LA BRTEN NAS, ,

ZAB LAM RIN CHEN GTER GYI SGO PHYES TE, ,ZAB DON ZUNG 'JUG

NOR BU 'DREN MKHAS KHYOD, ,ZAB LAM RDO RJE THEG PA'I KHYAB BDAG

NYID, ,RAB TU DBEN PA'I RI BO'I BA GAM LAS, ,RAB 'BYAMS

GSUNGS RAB NYAMS SU BSTAR BA'I MTHUS, ,RAB MANG RTOGS PA'I

'OD SNANG 'BUM SPROS PAS, ,RAB GSAL NAM MKHA'I NOR BU'ANG

MOG POR GYUR, ,ZHES BLA GO RDO RJE 'CHANG ZHES YONGS SU GRAGS PA

RJE BTZUN 'JIGS MED 'PHRIN LAS RGYA MTSO DPAL BZANG BO'I RNAM

PAR THAR BA DAD PA'I PADMO BZHAD PA'I BDEN GTAM NYI MA GZHON

NU ZHES BYA BA LAS THA MAR NYIN MTSAN KUN TU NYAMS SU BLANGS TE

NYAMS DANG RTOGS PA GONG DU 'PHEL BA'I SARGA STE GSUM PA'O, ,

BSTAN 'GRO'I DON RLABS CHEN MDZAD PA'I SARGA,

RAB 'JIGS NYON SHES SGRIB PA'I GRONG KHYER DAG ,GZHOM

@069 MED BDE CHEN ZHO 'THUNG RUS PAS BCOM, ,'PHRIN LAS RNAM

BZHI'I RIN CHEN KYO BA YIS, ,GDUL BYA RGYA MTSO 'DREN PA'I MGON

DES SKYONGS, ,THOS DON GDAMS PAR SHAR BA'I NYAMS LEN DAG ,

CHU SHEL DBANG BO GCIG TU LEGS BZLUMS NAS, ,GZHAN PHAN GA

BUR ZEGS MA 'BUM SPROS PAS, ,THUB BSTAN RGYA MTSO SPEL BA'I

BYUNG BA BRJOD, ,BZHI BA DE DAG KUN KYANG BSTAN PA RIN PO CHE

RGYAS PA'I CHED DU BSNGOS TE CHOS KYI 'KHOR LO BSKOR CING BYA BA LAS

KYI 'KHOR LO'I SGO NAS KYANG BSTAN 'GRO'I DON RLABS CHEN MDZAD PA

NI, SKU BSNYUNG ZHIG BZHES PA'I SKABS GUNG THANG BLO GROS ZHES YONGS

SU GRAGS PA'I DGE BSHES CHEN PO DES KHA DAR ZHIG BSKUR TE ZHAL

'DON GYI SKABS SOGS SU RANG GI SKU TSE BRTAN PA'I CHED DU DMIGS

NA LEGS TSUL GSUNGS PA BZHIN SNYAN BSKUL ZHUS PAR ZHAL NAS,

NGA'I TSE GANG BO 'DIR KHA 'DON DANG DGE SPYOR GANG BYAS THAMS

CAD TSE 'DI'I CHED DU DMIGS NAS BTON MA MYONG, ,ZHES

GSUNGS, DE LTAR THOS BSAM SGOM GSUM GANG BYAS THAMS CAD

BSTAN PA RIN PO CHE RGYAS PA'I CHED DU BSNGO BAR MDZAD PA NI, RJE

BDAG NYID CHEN POS, KUN KYANG BSTAN PA RGYAS PA'I CHED DU

BSNGOS, ,ZHES GSUNGS PA LTAR SANGS RGYAS DANG BYANG CHUB SEMS

DPA'I MDZAD PA KHO NA'O, ,DE LTAR GZHAN SEMS CAN GYI DON

@070 'BA' ZHIG THUGS LA DGONGS PA NA, KUN MKHYEN 'JIGS MED

DBANG BO'I ZHAL NAS, MI ZAD SRID PA'I 'BROG DGON NYAM NGA

BAR, ,SDUG BSNGAL KHUR GYIS DUB PA'I 'GRO RNAMS LA, ,PHAN

DANG BDE BA'I YAL 'DAB KUN RDZOGS PA'I, ,GRIB BSIL CHOS

DANG MTSUNGS PA YOD MA YIN, ,ZHES DANG, MDZAD PA KUN

LAS GSUNG GI NI, ,MDZAD PA MCHOG YIN, ,ZHES DANG, CHOS

NYID BDEN PA BSTAN PAS GROL BAR 'GYUR, ,ZHES GSUNGS PA

LTAR 'GRO BA RNAMS 'KHOR BA LAS SGROL BYED KYI THABS DNGOS NI RGYU

'BRAS KYI THEG PA GNYIS KYIS BSDUS PA'I DAM PA'I CHOS STON PA KHO

NA YIN NO, ,DE'I SKABS THAMS CAD MKHYEN PA SGO MANG MKHAN

RIN PO CHE BLO BZANG TSUL KHRIMS RGYA MTSO'I ZHAL NAS, BKA' 'GYUR

GYI LUNG NGAS THOB KYANG MA THOB, THOB KYANG 'DON MI NUS, KHYOD

KYIS THON DANG LEGS ZHES BSKUL BA DANG, YANG NYIN GCIG SKYABS

MGON THAMS CAD MKHYEN PA RJE BSKAL BZANG THUB BSTAN DBANG

PHYUG GIS KHA DAR CHE LEGS SHIG BSKUR TE GZHUNG BAR LO BSTAR

CHAGS SU LAM RIM BDE LAM DANG 'JAM DPAL ZHAL LUNG GI KHRID

RES MOS SU GNANG BA'I SROL YOD PA MI NUB PAR SKYONGS DGOS ZHES

BSTAN PA'I BDAG POR MNGA' GSOL BA DANG, ZHANG STON CHOS KYI

RGYAL BOS, KHYOD KYIS BTON NA NGA DGA' GSUNGS NAS SBAS DON

@071 KUN GSAL GYI BSHAD LUNG GNANG BCUG SGO MANG RDO RJE 'CHANG BLO

BZANG TSUL KHRIMS RGYA MTSOS, BKA' 'GYUR GYI LUNG GNANG BA SHIN

TU LEGS, DE BZHIN DU PHYIS SU'ANG BKA' CHOS 'CHAD SPEL RGYA

CHEN GNANG DGOS TSUL SOGS BKA' BSKUL GNANG BA LA SOGS

PAR BRTEN NAS DAM PA'I CHOS KYI 'KHOR LO RGYUN MI 'CHAD PAR

BSKOR BA YIN TE RAGS RIM ZHIG BRJOD NA, BKA' 'GYUR TSAR

GCIG BSTAN 'GYUR LUNG RGYUN GANG YOD TSAR GSUM, RJE YAB

SRAS GSUNG 'BUM TSAR BZHI RE, 'DUL 'DZIN DANG RJE DGE 'DUN

GRUB KYI GSUNG 'BUM YANG TSAR BZHI, LHO BRAG BKA' 'BUM,

DBEN SA BKA' 'BUM, RGYAL DBANG BDUN PA'I GSUNG 'BUM,

LCANG SKYA GONG MA NGAG DBANG CHOS LDAN DANG, LCANG SKYA ROL BA'I RDO

RJE'I GSUNG 'BUM, KLONG RDOL GSUNG 'BUM, KHYA DGE BLO GROS RGYA

MTSO DANG, PAn CHEN BSTAN PA'I NYI MA, RGYAL MKHAN PO GRAGS

PA RGYAL MTSAN RNAMS KYI GSUNG 'BUM TSAR GNYIS RE, PAn CHEN

BLO BZANG CHOS RGYAN GYI GSUNG 'BUM TSAR GSUM, DPON SLOB

BYAMS PA'I GSUNG 'BUM TSAR BZHI, KUN MKHYEN GONG MA'I GSUNG

'BUM TSAR BDUN, KUN MKHYEN 'JIGS MED DBANG BO'I GSUNG

'BUM MTSAR BZHI, GUNG THANG BSTAN PA'I SGRON ME'I GSUNG 'BUM

TSAR DRUG AA KHU RIN PO CHE SHES RAB RGYA MTSO'I GSUNG 'BUM TSAR

@072 BCU GSUM, AA KHU RIN PO CHE ZHANG STON BSTAN PA RGYA MTSO'I GSUNG

'BUM TSAR DGU, MKHAS GRUB SANGS RGYAS YE SHES, ZHOG DON

YOD MKHAS GRUB 'JAM DBYANGS BDE BA'I RDO RJE, THU'U BKVAN CHOS

KYI NYI MA, DBAL MANG PAndI TA, MKHAN RIN PO CHE NGAG DBANG THUB

BSTAN RGYA MTSO RNAMS KYI GSUNG 'BUM TSAR RE RE, SNGAGS PHYOGS

PO TI, CHOS SPYOD RAB GSAL SOGS LUNG PHRAN SHIN TU MANG BAS

GRANGS KYIS MI ZIN BKA' GDAMS GLEGS BAM TSAR BCU, MA nI

BKA' 'BUM DANG, MI LA'I MGUR 'BUM TSAR DRUG RE STE RANG

RANG GI GRANGS TSAD BSHAD PA LAS MI NYUNG BA LHAG KYANG MCHIS

GSUNGS, BSHAD LUNG GI SKOR LA, LAM RIN CHEN MO TSAR SUM

CUR NYE BA, LAM RIM CHUNG NGU TSAR BCO LNGA, SNGAGS RIM CHEN MO

TSAR NYI SHU, RIM LNGA GSAL SGRON, LEGS BSHAD SNYING BO, GRUB

MTHA' RTZA 'GREL, LAM RIM MCHAN BZHI MA, RJE'I BSTOD PA DON

LDAN MA RTZA 'GREL LAN MANG POR GSUNGS, 'GREL BA BZHI SBRAGS

TSAR BDUN, DUS 'KHOR 'GREL CHEN TSAR GSUM, SBAS DON

KUN GSAL TSAR NYI SHU, BSKYED RIM DNGOS GRUB RGYA MTSO TSAR

BRGYAD DAM DGU, RANG GIS GANG THOB PA RNAMS YANG YANG BTON

PAS GRANGS MI ZIN GSUNGS, KHRID KYI SKOR BDE LAM TSAR BZHI

BCU, 'JAM DPAL ZHAL LUNG TSAR NYI SHU LHAG GSANG BDE

@073 'JIGS GSUM GYI BSKYED RDZOGS TSAR SUM CU RE, MKHA' SPYOD

BSKYED RDZOGS TSAR BZHI BCU LAS MI NYUNG GSUNGS, KHRID CHUNG GI

SKOR RNAMS BGRANGS KYIS MI LANG, BLA MCHOD DANG PHYAG CHEN YANG

MANG DU GNANG, SRAD RGYUD BLA MA'I RNAL 'BYOR, GTOR MA BRGYA

RTZA TSAR BRGYAD CU LHAG MDOR DRIL NA LO GCIG GI KHONGS NA BKA'

CHOS MED PA NYIN NYI SHU LAS MED PA MANG GSUNGS LA, 'DI DAG

NI DGUNG LO NYI SHU RTZA GRANGS NAS LNGA BCU MA ZIN PA'I BAR GYI ZIN

THO LTAR YIN LA, DGUNG LO LNGA BCU NAS BRGYAD CU GYA GRANGS BAR

DU'ANG BKA' CHOS RGYUN MI CHAD PAR GNANG BA DANG, SPYI ZUR GYI

DBANG DANG RJES GNANG, SGOM LUNG RIGS GTAD SROG GTAD

SOGS GRANGS KYIS MI LANG LA, CHE LONG TZAM ZHIG NI SKU TSE 'DI NYID

KYI RNAM THAR THAR CHAGS SU 'GOD PA'I SKABS SU BSHAD PAR BYA'O, ,

DE LTAR BKA' CHOS BAR MA CHAD PAR GNANG BA MA ZAD, BYA

BA LAS KYI 'KHOR LO'I SGO NAS KYANG RGYAL BSTAN SPEL BA NI, DGUNG

LO NGA GSUM PA SA RTA LOR SNGAR CHOS SKYONG GI LUNG BSTAN DU, PHRAG

DOG GYA GYU'I DRI BZHON 'TSUB MA NAS, ,ZHE SDANG DU BA'I RGYAL

MTSAN 'DZIN PA YIS, ,GTI MUG GNYIS 'THUNG BSKYON PA'I NA

BA STE, ,NGA RGYAL RI BO 'BIGS BYED DRAG TU 'BEBS, ,ZHES

GSUNGS PA DUS SU BAB STE RGYA HOS KYI 'KHRUG ZING LA BRTEN PHYI NANG

@074 KUN TU ZING LONG BYUNG TSE DGON BKRA SHIS 'KHYIL 'JIG LA KHAD PA'I

DUS SU, RIGS GSUM SGYU 'PHRUL BLO BZANG GRAGS PA DANG, ,

'JAM DBYANGS BZHAD PA'I SKU TSE PHRENG BRGYUD KYI, ,RMAD BYUNG

THUGS BSKYED BDEN PA'I MTHU BYIN GYIS, ,NAG PHYOGS GDUG

PA'I BSAM SBYOR ZHI BAR MDZOD, ,CES GSUNGS NAS ZHAL SLOB

RNAMS LA LUNG GNANG STE BTON PA DANG, RGYA HOS DPON LA GUS

ZOL SOGS THABS MKHAS DANG, THUGS RIM SNA TSOGS MDZAD PA'I

RKYEN LAS DGON SDE BKRA SHIS 'KHYIL 'DIR NANG KHAG RE GNYIS RE

LA NYES SKYON BYUNG BA LAS GZHAN, DGON SPYI GRA MA NYAMS PAR

CHAGS THUB PA BYUNG BA'ANG RJE 'DI BA'I 'PHRIN LAS KHO NA YIN, KHONG

GI GSUNG LAS, DGON GRA MA CHAG PA ZHIG BYUNG BAS NYIN MTSAN

KUN TU SEMS LA BCANGS RGYU TSE GCIG LA GO CHOD PA GCIG PUR

SEMS YOD CES GSUNGS, YANG GRVA JA'I TSOGS ZANGS BCAG PA

THUGS KYIS MA BZOD PAR DNGUL RDO TSAD DRUG GIS TSOGS ZANGS

BSGRUBS, LHA MO BDE CHEN GYI CHOS THOG CIG NYAMS PA GSO BA'I

PHYIR DNGUL SRANG SUM BRGYA DANG DNGOS PO 'BOR CHEN SBYOR 'JAGS

MDZAD, SHING LE KHAR DUS 'KHOR GSAR 'DZUGS CHED DNGUL SRANG

DRUG CU DANG, DONG TSE KHRON NYIS BRGYA DANG RAS SOGS SBYOR

'JAGS DANG BRGYA MCHOD PHUL BA SOGS MANG, CHOS DPAL ZHING

@075 DU DNGUL RDO TSAD NYI SHUS JO KHANG BZHENGS, RDO SBIS GZHUNG LA GRO

'JAGS DRUG NAS 'JAGS BRGYA DANG NYI SHU, DONG TZE THO'U KHRON

NYIS STONG DANG NYIS BRGYA MCHOD RTEN BZHENGS RGYU'I THEBS SU

BZHAG PHYIS SU ZHIG GSOS THEBS LA 'BRU BRE LNGA BRGYA DANG DNGUL

SGOR BRGYA GNANG, BYA KHYUNG DU DGE 'DUN RE RE'I PHYAG TU DONG TZE

KHRON BDUN RE PHUL, PHYIS SU'ANG LAN GNYIS SU 'GYED BTANG,

KHONG GI 'KHRUNGS YUL DU MCHOD RTEN CHEN PO ZHIG BZHENGS YOD PA

DE'I NYI ZLA ZAR TSAGS KYI CHED DNGUL SGOR CHIG STONG DRUG BRGYA

GNANG, ZHONG SHAN JO BO LA BZANG GOS YUG GNYIS LAS GRUB PA'I

RNAM SBYAR KHYAD 'PHAGS DANG, DNGUL GYI 'KHOR LO 'PHRENG RGYAN ZAR

TSAGS CAN DANG SPOS DMAR GYI MGUL 'PHRENG SOGS PHUL, SER

'BRAS SOGS DBUS PHYOGS KYI GRVA SA THAMS CAD DU MI MNGAGS NAS

DGON SDE THAMS CAD LA GTONG SGO GNANG BA DANG, DGUNG LO BZHI

BCU ZHE GRANGS YAR MAR ZHIG NAS LO RE BZHIN THOS BSAM GLING LA

GRVA JA RE GTONG BAR MDZAD PA SOGS PHYOGS RIS MED KYI DGE 'DUN

RNAMS LA PHOG 'GYED GNANG STE THAMS CAD BSTAN PA RIN PO CHE RGYAS

PA'I CHED DU BSNGOS PA BGRANGS KYIS MI LONGS LA 'GA' ZHIG RNAM

THAR THAR CHAGS SU 'GOD PA'I SKABS SU GSAL, LHA KHANG GTZUG

LAG KHANG BZHENGS PA'I SKOR LA, TSOGS CHEN 'DU KHANG GI GTZANG

@076 KHANG RGYA BSKYED DANG, 'DU KHANG STENG 'OG KHYAMS DANG BCAS PA

LA TSON RGYAN GSAR BAS SPRAS SHING, RGYA GAR NAG LAS BYUNG BA'I

BZANG GOS KYI 'PHAN DANG RGYAL MTSAN SOGS MCHOD RDZAS 'DU KHANG

GANG BA BZHAG NANG RTEN YANG RJE'I LHA KHANG GI NANG RTEN RJE'I SKU

BRNYAN CHEN PO NI BSTAN PA'I GEGS CHAG GI DBANG GIS YANG DANG

YANG DU ME SKYON SOGS KYI DBANG GIS MA 'GRUB PAR LUS PA THUGS

KYIS MA BZOD PAR GZHI NAS SMAN SKU CHEN PO THOG TSAD GNYIS CAN

GSAR BZHENGS MDZAD, LHA BZO KUN SPANGS GNAS BRTAN PA DANG

LHAN DU DBU NI KHONG GIS PHYAG BZO GNANG ZHING, THIG RTZA SOGS

BZO LAS KUN LA LHA BZO DANG MNYAM DU PHYAG LAS GNANG, GZUNGS

GZHUGS LA BKA' BSTAN GNYIS, GSUNG 'BUM CHES MANG PO

SOGS RTEN BSAM GYIS MI KHYAB PAS GTAMS, GZHAN YANG NYE

SRAS BRGYAD DANG BYAMS 'JAM DBYANGS 'JAM DPAL SMRA SENG GI SKU

LUGS SU BLUGS PA KHRI TSAD MA STONG LHAG DANG GYAN THANG DU MA BCAS

SOGS BZHENGS, GZHAN SKU BZHENGS PA'I SDOM GRANGS NI, DGUNG

LO BCO BRGYAD THOG RDO RJE 'CHANG NGAG DBANG THUB BSTAN RGYA MTSO,

MKHAN RIN PO CHE BLO BZANG TSUL KHRIMS RGYA MTSO, BDE MCHOG

MKHA' SPYOD MA, KHROS NAG ZHAL BZHI BA RNAMS KYI TZA KA LI RE

BZHENGS, AA LAGS MKHAN RIN PO CHE NGAG DBANG THUB BSTAN RGYA

@077 MTSO'I NA BZA'I STENG DU RJE'I SKU ZHIG DANG, BDE GSANG 'JIGS

GSUM GYI DKYIL 'KHOR RNAMS BZHENGS PA RTEN BZHENGS GYI THOG MA

RED, PHYI NAS 'JAM DBYANGS DMAR SER, THUGS RJE CHEN PO

RGYAL BRGYA MTSO, DUS 'KHOR THANG SKU CHE CHUNG GNYIS, BDE BA CAN

GYI ZHING BKOD, GYAN THANG GCIG BSHAGS LHA SO LNGA GCIG THANG

GNYIS, GSUM THANG GNYIS, BRGYAD THANG GCIG SMAN SKU TSAN

GNYIS BSDOMS PAS YONGS RDZOGS BDUN, BDE MCHOG GI THANG GA

CHE BA, MGON CHOS 'JIGS GSUM GYI THANG GA CHE BA RE RE, DNGUL

RDO TSAD BZHI LAS BSGRUBS PA'I RDO'I SKU DBU RGYAN RIN PO CHE DU MAS

SPRAS PA RANG GI LUS TSAD CAN 'DI BLA BRANG RGYUD KHANG STENG DU

BZHUGS, GNAS BCU DGU THANG KHYAD MTSAR ZHIG CHOS DPAL ZHING

TSOGS CHEN 'DU KHANG DU BZHUGS, YANG GNAS BCU BDUN THANG

DGON DE'I RGYUD KHANG DU BZHUGS, YANG GNAS BCU'I THANG GA NYER

GSUM CAN KHYAD 'PHAGS DANG, BYAMS PA'I GOS SKU BCAS DE

KA'I GZIM KHANG DU BZHUGS, SLAR YANG BDUN THANG GCIG

RNAMS BSDOMS PAS TSAR BZHI, RDO RJE SEMS DPA' DANG, 'JAM

DBYANGS KYI THANG GA CHE BA, SMAN BLA'I ZHING BKOD KHYAD MTSAR TE

GSUM PO DE KA'I SMAN PA'I 'DU KHANG DU BZHUGS, RDO RJE MI 'KHRUGS

PA'I THANG GA CHE LEGS DE KA'I RI KHROD DU BZHUGS, RJE RIN PO CHE

@078 TZONG KHA BRGYAD CU'I ZHAL THANG BCO LNGA GONG BSHAM ZHAL KHEB SOGS

BSDOMS PAS DNGUL RDO TSAD RE RE SONG PA 'DI BLA BRANG TSOGS CHEN

'DU KHANG DU BZHUGS, YANG RJE TZONG KHA BRGYAD CU GONG GSHAM

ZHAL KHEB SPUS LEGS CAN GYI THANG GA BCO LNGA SMAN PA'I 'DU KHANG DU

BZHUGS, RDO RJE MI 'KHRUGS PA'I GSER SKU CHE LEGS SHIG KYANG

DER BZHAG PHYAG RDOR 'KHOR CHEN GYI THANG SKU CHE LEGS GCIG BLA

BRANG RGYUD KHANG DU BZHAG TSE LHA RNAM GSUM RANG GI LUS TSAD DANG

MNYAM PA'I THANG GA CHE BA GSUM, YANG DE 'DRA'I TSE DPAG MED

GCIG STE BZHI, RGYAN DRUG MCHOG GNYIS, RTA MGRIN, TSE DPAG

MED, DGA' LDAN LHA BRGYA MA SOGS BSDOMS PAS THANG GA CHE CHUNG

SUM CUR NYE BA HOR TSANG DGON GSAR DU BZHAG YANG DGON DER

'OD DPAG MED KYI ZHING BKOD GYAN THANG SPUS LEGS GCIG BZHAG

SKU PHYOGS 'KHRUNGS RABS SOGS THANG GA CHE CHUNG NYI SHU BLA BRANG RGYUD

KHANG DU BZHAG RDO RJE 'JIGS BYED KYI SMAN SKU CHE BA GCIG DANG,

THANG GA BYIN CAN ZHIG RGYUD KHANG STENG DU BZHUGS, MGON CHOS

'JIGS GSUM GYI ZHAL THANG CHE BA MTHA' SHAN SPUS LEGS SGROL

DKAR LI MA KHRI TZE GSUM CAN, RJE RIN PO CHE'I LI MA KHRI TZE DO, RDO

RJE MI 'KHRUGS PA KHRI TZE DO, RJE RIN PO CHE DANG SGROL MA'I SMAN SKU

BYON LEGS RNAMS KVA RING DGON DU BZHUGS, SHING LE KHAR GUR

@079 MGON GSAR BZHENGS DANG, GONG GI DUS 'KHOR GYI THANG SKU CHE BA

BZHAG SHEL DGON DU RGYAL BA RDO RJE 'CHANG LA GRUB CHEN BRGYAD CUS

BSKOR BA'I THANG GA CHE BA GONG GSHAM ZHAL KHEB BCAS SPUS LEGS

SHIG BZHAG BIS MDO DGON DU THUB SKU GSER ZANGS LAS GRUB

PA TSON DGU BA ZHIG BZHAG SE CHANG DGON DU JO'I SKU KHRI RGYAB YOL

CAN ZHIG BZHAG HOR TSANG TZAG TZAG DGON PAR DNGUL RDO TSAD

LNGA LAS GRUB PA'I KUN RIG DANG, 'OD DPAG MED, MI 'KHRUGS PA

THOG TSAD PHYED DANG GNYIS PA CAN RE BZHENGS, CHOS DPAL ZHING GI

GZIM KHANG DU STON PA, SGROL DKAR, 'JAM DBYANGS DKAR BO

GSUM RANG GI LUS TSAD CAN RE BZHENGS, DES MTSON GZIM KHANG

DER LI MA DANG SMAN SKU BSDOMS PAS SKU BRNYAN CHE CHUNG BRGYA DANG

DON BDUN BZHUGS, YANG MGON PO'I SKU LI MA KHRI TZE GSUM

CAN, DNGUL RDO TSAD DRUG GIS BLUS PA'I SGROL MA NYER GCIG DNGUL

SRANG BRGYA DANG DON GSUM GYIS BSGRUBS PA'I SGROL LJANG GTZO 'KHOR

GSUM, SGROL MA KHRI TSAD CAN RNAMS GZIM KHANG DER BZHUGS,

DGUNG LO ZHE DGU YAN GYI SKU BRNYAN LI MA DANG SMAN SKU BCAS DRUG

CU LHAG BLA BRANG RGYUD KHANG DU BZHUGS, BLA BRANG TSOGS CHEN 'DU

KHANG GI RGYA MTHONG GI LOGS RIS THAMS CAD TSVAS ZOS TE CHUD 'DZA'

BA THUGS KYIS MA BZOD PAR SNGON MA JI BZHIN BZHENGS NAS LEGS

@080 MDZES SU BSGRUBS PA DE LA GYAN THANG DGU YOD PAS RE RE LA DNGUL

SRANG SUM CU SO DRUG RE YON DU PHUL, CHOS DPAL ZHING DU DUS

'KHOR GRVA TSANG DU DNGUL SGOR DRUG CU RE LNGAS DUS KYI 'KHOR LO'I SKU

MI TSAD TZAM BZHENGS TE BZHAG PA DANG, DNGUL SGOR STONG PHRAG

GSUM GYIS SANGS RGYAS STONG SKU BZHENGS SHING LOG RIS KYI THEBS

SU'ANG DNGUL SRANG DRUG CU PHUL, BLA BRANG BRTZAN KHANG DU GYAN THANG

GSUM BZHAG RGAN RGYA'I BAN RGYAR THANG GA GSUM BZHAG NAS LTUNG

BSHAGS BTZUGS, GZHAN YANG GTONG RTZA BZHAG THO NI, MTSO KHAR

BZANG SPYOD 'DON RGYUN LA KHRON LNGA BCU DANG 'BRU 'JAGS BZHI,

HOR TSANG TZAG TZAG DGON PAR BZANG SPYOD GSAR BTZUGS KYI

THEBS LA KHRON DRUG BRGYA DANG NAS BRE NYIS BRGYA, BKRA SHIS SGAR DU

BDE MCHOG BDAG 'JUG GSAR BTZUGS KYI RTEN KHRON BRGYA DANG LNGA

BCU, KHA GYA'I SGAR RNYING DU LTUNG BSHAGS PHYAG MCHOD GSAR

BTZUGS LA KHRON BRGYA DANG NYI SHU, GSANG 'DUS BDAG 'JUG

GSAR TSUGS LA NAS BRE BZHI BRGYA, SGAR GSAR DU BYAMS KHANG GI

THEBS LA KHRON STONG, MDZOD DGE DME PO'I SGAR GSAR DU KHRON

STONG, CHAS PA RGYA MKHAR DGON ZHIG GSOS 'THEB LA DNGUL SGOR

SUM BRGYA DANG GOS SER BO KHA BCU, RJE MI LA'I SKU TSON LNGA CAN,

DNGUL GYI MCHOD RTEN DANG SGROL DKAR LI MA KHRI TZE GANG RE, SA

@081 DMAR DGON PA ZHIG GSOS CHED THO'I KHRON BRGYA DANG BCO LNGA,

DNGUL RI'I SER SDER LTUNG BSHAGS GSAR BTZUGS LA MCHOD 'THEB

LNGA BCU, MAR ME'I RKONG BU BRGYA, DNGUL SRANG DON LNGA, BLA BRANG

LO RNYING LCAGS MKHAR GYI 'THEB LA KHRON STONG DANG BRGYAD BRGYA BZHAG

GZHAN YANG SA BON DU MA THEBS PA DU MA YOD DE DPER NA, DMU

DGE BKRA SHIS 'KHOR LO'I DGON DU BKA' 'GYUR SNAR THANG DPAR

MA TSAR GCIG GNANG BA DANG, RJE YAB SRAS KYI GSUNG 'BUM SOGS

SMRAS PA, THOS BSAM SGOM PA'I RIN CHEN RDUL MANG LAS, ,NYER

@082 BZLOG ,THABS SHES GSER GYI CHU 'DZIN STUG PO LAS, ,DAM CHOS

SPRIN GYI ME TOG 'BUM PHAB STE, ,LOG RTOG ZHUGS CHEN GZHIL DANG

BAS, ,NGA LAS NU YI GRAGS PA ZIL GYIS MNAN, ,ZHES BLA GO RDO RJE

'CHANG ZHES YONGS SU GRAGS PA RJE BTZUN 'JIGS MED 'PHRIN LAS

RGYA MTSO DPAL BZANG BO'I RNAM PAR THAR BA DAD PA'I PADMO BZHAD

PA'I BDEN GTAM NYI MA GZHON NU ZHES BYA BA LAS THOG MTHA' BAR

GSUM GYI DGE TSOGS KUN KYANG BSTAN PA RGYAS PA'I CHED DU BSNGOS

TE CHOS KYI 'KHOR LO BSKOR CING, BYA BA LAS KYI 'KHOR LO'I SGO NAS

KYANG BSTAN 'GRO'I DON RLABS CHEN MDZAD PA'I SARGA STE BZHI BA'O, ,

GNYIS BA SKU TSE 'DI NYID KYI RNAM THAR RAGS RIM THAR CHAGS SU 'GOD PA,

@083 'CHI MED BYE BA'I MGON DU GYUR, ,'PHRIN LAS LHUN 'GRUB GA

BUR 'BUM 'DZAG PA, ,THUB BSTAN RGYA MTSO SPEL BA'I DPAL DU

GYUR, ,CHOS SKU'I RANG GZUGS BYE BA BRGYA STONG LAS, ,ZHING

'DIR GSUM LDAN NGUR SMRIG RNAM ROL BA'I, ,BYUNG BA RIN CHEN

NGO MTSAR 'BUM PHRAG DAG ,SNYAN PA'I TSIG GI SRAD BUR BRGYU BAR

RAGS RIM THAR CHAGS SU 'GOD PA LA,

SKU BLTAMS SHING MTSAN GYI ME TOG RGYAS TE GONG MA'I

@098 ZHABS RDUL SPYI BOR BSTEN PA'I SKAL BZANG THOB STE BSTAN PA'I

'JUG SGO SKYABS 'GRO'I KHRID DANG, DGA' LDAN LHA BRGYA MA DANG,

GANG BLO MA SOGS LUNG PHRAN KHA YAR THOB GSUNGS, DE SKABS LO'I

'BRUG SKAD THOG MAR BYUNG BAS RTEN 'BREL LEGS ZHES PHEBS,

NYUNG SHAS 'BRI BA'I PHYAG G-YOG ZHU BA SOGS KYI SKAL BA'ANG THOB

GZHUNG RGYUGS PHUL,

DGUNG GRANGS BCU BDUN PA RAB TSES CHU PHO RTA'I LOR GZHUNG

GSAR DU SLEBS NAS DGE 'DUN NYI SHU GSAR RTZOD DANG DUS 'GRIG

PAS ZLA GNYIS PA'I NYER DRUG GI BAR CHOS GRVAR PHEBS, DE SKABS

DGE RGAN TSANG NAS DA KHYOD AA LAGS RIN PO CHE NAS BKA' 'GYUR

GYI LUNG GNANG BA NYAN DU SONG, THE'U BLO BZANG GI GAM NAS SDOD

LA DPE LTAS KYANG LE SHOR MED PA GYIS ZHES GSUNGS PA LTAR BKA'

@099 PAS RA DUM PA NAS BZUNG RDZOGS PAR NYAN, SNGON STAG GE TSANG

NAS KHYOD TSOGS CHOS 'GRIM PA LA KHANG MIG CHUNG NGU ZHIG GIS YONG

GSUNGS PA LTAR, 'DI LOR KHANG BA SNGA MA BTZONG STE KHANG CHUNG ZHIG

TU SPOS, DE PHYIN KHA SMRAS GLENG BRJOD MANG BA SOGS DANG YANG

DGOS KHAMS MA SNYOMS PAR BRTEN GRO RA TSANG MO MA RNO SHOS SU

GRAGS PAS BRTAG PA ZHUS PAR, RTA MGRIN GYI BSNYEN PA DANG GUR

DRAG DANG RTA MGRIN 'KHOR LO SHAM BU CAN YOD PAS DE SKOR ZER,

DE 'PHRAL KHONG RANG NYID RTA MGRIN GYI BSNYEN PAR BZHUGS PA'I

MNAL LAM DU KHONG DANG KHONG GI 'DZIN GRVA BCAS BSDUS CHEN GYI GO

SAR RTZOD PA BYED PA LA KHONG AA LAGS RIN PO CHE GLO BUR DU PHEBS

BYUNG BA ZHAL DMAR ZHING ZIL CHE BA KHRO TSUL GYIS SPYAN HRIG HRIG

PHYOGS KUN GZIGS PAS KHONG GI 'DZIN GRVA'I SMAD SOG MA CIG ZER

BA DE LA BRDUNG RDEG MANG BO GNANG BA ZHIG RMIS, BSNYEN PA GROL

TSE KHAMS KYANG RANG SAR CUNG BABS, 'KHOR LO DE 'BAD PAS

BSKOR BAS THAMS CAD NAS PHYI PHYIR MI 'TSAM PAR GYUR BAS 'KHOR

LOS LAN PAR SHES NAS GZHAN LA BYIN, LHA KHYAD PAR BA YIN NGES

LA NGED RANG LA SNGA 'GYUR PHYOGS 'DI LA LAS 'PHRO NGAN PAS 'BREL

MED PA GO GSUNGS, RDO RJE 'CHANG MKHAN RIN PO CHE NGAG DBANG

DGE LEGS TSANG NGAG DBANG THUB BSTAN RGYA MTSO DE NYID KYIS DUS

@100 'KHOR DBANG SKUR SKABS SDE KHRI SPRUL BA'I SKU 'JIGS MED BSTAN

PA'I NYI MA TSANG NAS KHONG LA NGED RANG GNYIS SHAMBHA LAR MNYAM 'GRO

ZHIG GNANG BAR KHYOD BLA RGAN SMA RA DKAR PO CAN ZHIG TU MA GYUR
